# Chapter-00.1: Roadmap to Learn React.js

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Beginner ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Advanced ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ React.js ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¶‡¶Æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶´‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ üí°

---

## üü¢ 1. Prerequisites (React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá)

React ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:

- **HTML5** (Semantic tags, Forms, Table ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø)
- **CSS3** (Flexbox, Grid, Animation, Responsive Design)
- **JavaScript (ES6+)**

  - let, const, arrow functions
  - template literals
  - array methods (map, filter, reduce)
  - destructuring
  - spread/rest operator
  - promises, async/await
  - modules & imports/exports

- **Basic Git & GitHub** (Version control)
- **Basic Terminal/Command Line** usage

---

## üü° 2. React Fundamentals

1. **Introduction to React**

   - React ‡¶ï‡ßÄ, ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü
   - SPA (Single Page Application) ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ

2. **Create React App / Vite** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Project Setup
3. **JSX**: JSX Syntax, Expressions, Attributes
4. **Components & Props**

   - Functional Components
   - Props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞
   - Props Drilling

5. **State & setState** (useState Hook)
6. **Handling Events**

   - onClick, onChange, onSubmit

7. **Conditional Rendering**

   - if-else
   - ternary operator

8. **Lists & Keys**

   - Array.map() ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá list render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

9. **Styling in React**

   - CSS Module
   - Inline Styles
   - Styled Components / Tailwind (optional)

---

## üü† 3. Intermediate Topics

1. **Hooks in Detail**

   - useEffect
   - useRef
   - useContext
   - Custom Hooks

2. **Context API** (Props Drilling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®)
3. **Forms & Controlled Components**
4. **React Router**

   - Routing
   - Nested Routes
   - useParams, useNavigate

5. **Fetching Data**

   - Fetch API / Axios
   - Loading & Error State

6. **Performance Optimization**

   - React.memo
   - useCallback
   - useMemo

7. **React DevTools**

---

## üü§ 4. Advanced React

1. **State Management Libraries**

   - Redux Toolkit
   - Zustand / Jotai (alternative)

2. **TypeScript with React**
3. **Code Splitting & Lazy Loading** (React.lazy, Suspense)
4. **React Query / TanStack Query** (Server State Management)
5. **Next.js** (React Framework for SSR/SSG)
6. **Testing**

   - Jest
   - React Testing Library

---

## üü£ 5. Build & Deploy

1. **Environment Variables & .env**
2. **Build for Production** (npm run build)
3. **Deploy to Hosting**

   - Vercel / Netlify / GitHub Pages

### 1. What is React?

**ReactJS** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **JavaScript library** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user interfaces (UI) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **Single Page Applications (SPA)** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá web page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ dynamically update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page reload ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ React ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá **Facebook** ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡ß®‡ß¶‡ßß‡ß© ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º library ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example of a Simple React Component:

```jsx
function Welcome() {
  return <h1>Hello, React!</h1>;
}

export default Welcome;
```

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **Component-based Architecture**, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü, ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 1.1 Single Page Application (SPA) ‡¶ï‡¶ø?

**Single Page Application (SPA)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ web application, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø page load ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ interaction ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßÄ page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ dynamically update ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page reload ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Traditional multi-page applications ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã page ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø server ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® HTML file fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ SPA ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ React ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ SPA ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ web applications ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç seamless ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

#### Example:

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Traditional web application ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® section ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **React** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ dynamically update ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

---

### 1.2 Component-Based Architecture ‡¶ï‡¶ø?

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶∞ **component-based architecture**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶É‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá **components** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
function Navbar() {
  return (
    <nav>
      <ul>
        <li>Home</li>
        <li>About</li>
        <li>Contact</li>
      </ul>
    </nav>
  );
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Navbar** component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø Navbar component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã page ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® reflect ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø development process ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Why Use React?

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Efficient UI Updates**:
   - React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá user interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM** feature ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Example of Efficient UI Updates with Virtual DOM:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Counter() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Count: {count}</h1>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>Increment</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, **count** state ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ increment ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user **button** ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ **count** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶ø-‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá UI ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá update ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Example Without Virtual DOM:

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ traditional JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <title>Counter Example</title>
    <script>
      function increment() {
        var count = document.getElementById("count");
        count.innerHTML = parseInt(count.innerHTML) + 1;
      }
    </script>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>Count: <span id="count">0</span></h1>
    <button onclick="increment()">Increment</button>
  </body>
</html>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ **button** ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ manual DOM manipulation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßú application ‡¶è performance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã **Virtual DOM** ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ DOM ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø browser ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã structure ‡¶∞‡¶ø-‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ direct manipulation ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç memory-heavy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Why React‚Äôs Approach is Better:

- **Performance**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM** ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá traditional approach ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã DOM structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Maintainability**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **declarative syntax** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç automatic DOM update ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá complex UI ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Problems Without React

React ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ modern web applications ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá traditional DOM manipulation ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### 1) Manual DOM Manipulation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶§‡¶æ

Traditional JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements manually manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø DOM API (`getElementById`, `querySelector`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ page ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá interaction ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá UI complex ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§

#### Example Without React (Dynamic List):

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **To-Do List** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® items ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
  <head>
    <script>
      function addItem() {
        const list = document.getElementById("list");
        const newItem = document.createElement("li");
        const inputValue = document.getElementById("input").value;
        newItem.textContent = inputValue;
        list.appendChild(newItem);
        document.getElementById("input").value = "";
      }
    </script>
  </head>
  <body>
    <h1>To-Do List</h1>
    <input type="text" id="input" placeholder="Enter new item" />
    <button onclick="addItem()">Add</button>
    <ul id="list"></ul>
  </body>
</html>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ user ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® item ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá list ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® **`<li>`** element ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ DOM ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø manipulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ complex lists ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### 2) Poor Code Reusability

Traditional JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° reusability ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ UI element ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ redundancy ‡¶∏‡ßÉ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç bugs ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example Without React (Navbar):

```html
<nav>
  <ul>
    <li>Home</li>
    <li>About</li>
    <li>Contact</li>
  </ul>
</nav>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple **Navbar** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø similar navbar ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Traditional JavaScript ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø component-based architecture ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá UI element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 3) Complex State Management

Traditional JavaScript ‡¶è **state management** ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø page ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® DOM element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá synchronize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§

#### Example (Without React State):

```html
<input type="text" id="name" placeholder="Enter your name" />
<button onclick="updateGreeting()">Greet</button>
<h1 id="greeting">Hello,</h1>

<script>
  function updateGreeting() {
    const name = document.getElementById("name").value;
    document.getElementById("greeting").innerHTML = "Hello, " + name;
  }
</script>
```

---

#### Solution with React:

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **state management** feature ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ state handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá synchronize ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Greeting() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");

  return (
    <div>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={name}
        onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Enter your name"
      />
      <h1>Hello, {name}!</h1>
    </div>
  );
}

export default Greeting;
```

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, user input ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ greeting dynamically update ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **state** ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ UI render ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM manipulation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

---

### 4. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø declarative, efficient, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible JavaScript library, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø UI development ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶§ complex applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá dynamic content management ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **component-based architecture** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Virtual DOM**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI management ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Traditional JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º React development ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ large-scale applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-01.1: Library vs Framework

### Table of Contents:

1. [What is a Library?](#what-is-a-library)
2. [What is a Framework?](#what-is-a-framework)
3. [Key Differences Between Library and Framework](#key-differences-between-library-and-framework)
4. [Examples of Popular Libraries and Frameworks](#examples-of-popular-libraries-and-frameworks)
5. [When to Use a Library vs. a Framework](#when-to-use-a-library-vs-a-framework)
6. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

---

### 1. What is a Library?

**Library** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø code collection ‡¶¨‡¶æ package, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ functionalities ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ pre-written functions ‡¶¨‡¶æ methods ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º function ‡¶¨‡¶æ method call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé developer ‡¶á decide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á code ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **React** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø library, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user interface ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ React developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø functions ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ control developer ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. What is a Framework?

**Framework** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø complete structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ architecture, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü guideline ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç control ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Framework ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü rules ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç conventions ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø predefined code structure ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç application ‡¶è‡¶∞ control ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá framework ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá developer ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü parts ‡¶è code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

##### ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Angular** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø framework, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø complete structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ architecture ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Angular application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Angular ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® services, components, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modules ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Angular application ‡¶è‡¶∞ flow ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. Key Differences Between Library and Framework

| **Aspect**      | **Library**                                              | **Framework**                                          |
| --------------- | -------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------ |
| **Control**     | Developer control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º code ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá | Framework control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá application structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flow   |
| **Flexibility** | Developer ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø flexibility ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá                  | Framework ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü guideline ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º |
| **Usage**       | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø library import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º   | Framework application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá       |
| **Examples**    | React, Lodash, jQuery                                    | Angular, Vue.js, Django                                |

#### Explanation:

- **Control**: Library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá developer control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá function call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Framework ‡¶è control ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá framework ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, developer framework ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü rules ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§
- **Flexibility**: Library ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá developer ‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® library ‡¶è‡¶∞ code ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Framework ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá developer framework ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç guideline ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá code ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§
- **Usage**: Library ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: data manipulation, DOM manipulation) ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Framework ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application structure predefined ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Examples of Popular Libraries and Frameworks

#### Libraries:

1. **React** (JavaScript)
2. **Lodash** (JavaScript)
3. **jQuery** (JavaScript)
4. **NumPy** (Python)
5. **Pandas** (Python)

#### Frameworks:

1. **Angular** (JavaScript)
2. **Vue.js** (JavaScript)
3. **Django** (Python)
4. **Laravel** (PHP)
5. **Spring** (Java)

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã library developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ UI components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ flexibility ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Angular ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã framework ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç control ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. When to Use a Library vs. a Framework

#### When to Use a Library:

- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü part ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø code reusability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexibility ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ specific functionality ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® DOM manipulation (jQuery) ‡¶¨‡¶æ data manipulation (Lodash, Pandas) ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application structure ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ control ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§

#### When to Use a Framework:

- ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø complete application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç predefined structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç architecture ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø code organization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç application structure ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§
- ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø large-scale application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø scalable structure ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

**Library** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Framework** ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á software development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ tools, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç control ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡•§

- **Library** developer ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø flexibility ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç developer control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **Framework** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó architecture ‡¶¨‡¶æ structure ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç developer ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á structure ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Framework ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá control ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç application ‡¶è‡¶∞ flow manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã libraries ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Angular ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã frameworks ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application structure ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ nature ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç requirement ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá library ‡¶¨‡¶æ framework ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

## ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá - ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™

‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶á‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

**‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá:** ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

**‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá:** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ draft ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ original ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá compare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ original ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

Virtual DOM ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá!

---

## DOM ‡¶ï‡¶ø? - ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶ø

### ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º DOM

DOM ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Document Object Model‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ webpage ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç organize ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ structure‡•§

```html
<!-- ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ HTML -->
<html>
  <body>
    <div>
      <h1>‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü</h1>
      <p>‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø paragraph</p>
      <button>Click Me</button>
    </div>
  </body>
</html>
```

Browser ‡¶è‡¶á HTML ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ tree structure ‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

```
html
  ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ body
      ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ div
          ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ h1 ("‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü")
          ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ p ("‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø paragraph")
          ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ button ("Click Me")
```

‡¶è‡¶á tree structure ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶≤ DOM‡•§

### DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø

- Browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á DOM
- JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá DOM change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º
- DOM change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá webpage ‡¶è ‡¶§‡ßé‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º

---

## Real DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø?

### ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡ßß: ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞ (Slow)

```javascript
// ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ 100‡¶ü‡¶æ list item ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá
const list = document.getElementById("myList");

// ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá 100‡¶ü‡¶æ item change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá
for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
  list.children[i].innerHTML = `Item ${i} - Updated`;
  // ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ browser ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page re-calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá!
}
```

**‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá?**

- ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ change ‡¶è browser ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ calculate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
- Layout ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (Reflow)
- Elements ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ paint ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (Repaint)
- ‡¶è‡¶á process 100 ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ repeat ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º!

### ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡ß®: ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º Update

```javascript
// ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ shopping cart ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶®
function updateCart() {
  // Total amount ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá
  document.getElementById("total").innerHTML = "‡ß´‡ß¶‡ß¶ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ";

  // ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ browser ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
  // ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ element ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá
}
```

### ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡ß©: Memory ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞

Real DOM elements ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï memory ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï properties ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## Virtual DOM ‡¶ï‡¶ø? - ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º

### ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ

Virtual DOM ‡¶π‡¶≤ Real DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ **copy** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript object ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá computer ‡¶è‡¶∞ memory ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ browser ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ memory ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

### ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ

```javascript
// Real DOM (Browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶®)
<div>
  <h1>Hello World</h1>
  <button>Click</button>
</div>

// Virtual DOM (Memory ‡¶§‡ßá JavaScript object ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá)
{
  tag: 'div',
  children: [
    {
      tag: 'h1',
      text: 'Hello World'
    },
    {
      tag: 'button',
      text: 'Click'
    }
  ]
}
```

### Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø

- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ JavaScript object
- Browser ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ
- Memory ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá
- ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ create ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º
- Real DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ exact copy

---

## Virtual DOM ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá? - Step by Step

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ - Virtual DOM ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ step by step ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶¨‡ßã‡•§

### Step 1: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ (Initial Render)

**‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ React Component:**

```javascript
function MyComponent() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶Æ");

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: {name}</h1>
      <button onClick={() => setName("‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ")}>‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:**

1Ô∏è‚É£ **React Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:**

```javascript
// Virtual DOM Tree (Memory ‡¶§‡ßá)
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    {
      type: 'h1',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶Æ'
    },
    {
      type: 'button',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®',
      onClick: [Function]
    }
  ]
}
```

2Ô∏è‚É£ **React ‡¶è‡¶á Virtual DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Real DOM ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:**

```html
<!-- Browser ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® -->
<div>
  <h1>‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶Æ</h1>
  <button>‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®</button>
</div>
```

### Step 2: State Change ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ

**User button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá:**

1Ô∏è‚É£ **setName('‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ') call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º**

2Ô∏è‚É£ **React ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º state ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá**

3Ô∏è‚É£ **React component function ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**

### Step 3: ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø

**React ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:**

```javascript
// ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM Tree (Memory ‡¶§‡ßá)
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    {
      type: 'h1',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ'  // ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá!
    },
    {
      type: 'button',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®',
      onClick: [Function]
    }
  ]
}
```

### Step 4: ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ (Diffing)

**React ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ Virtual DOM tree ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:**

```javascript
// ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® Tree
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    {
      type: 'h1',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶Æ'     // ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶® value
    },
    // ... ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ same
  ]
}

// ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Tree
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    {
      type: 'h1',
      text: '‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ'     // ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® value
    },
    // ... ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨ same
  ]
}
```

**React ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:**

- `div` element same ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚úì
- `button` element same ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚úì
- ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `h1` ‡¶è‡¶∞ text ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‚ö°

### Step 5: Real DOM Update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ (Reconciliation)

**React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ Real DOM ‡¶è update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:**

```javascript
// React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ line execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
document.querySelector("h1").textContent = "‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ";

// ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ page ‡¶¨‡¶æ component ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ!
```

**Result:** Browser ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ h1 ‡¶è‡¶∞ text '‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶Æ' ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá '‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ' ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

## ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶ø

‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ shopping cart ‡¶è‡¶∞ example ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã process ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø:

### Initial State

```javascript
function ShoppingCart() {
  const [items, setItems] = useState([
    { id: 1, name: "‡¶Ü‡¶Æ", price: 100, quantity: 2 },
    { id: 2, name: "‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ", price: 50, quantity: 5 },
  ]);

  const total = items.reduce(
    (sum, item) => sum + item.price * item.quantity,
    0
  );

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Shopping Cart</h1>
      <ul>
        {items.map((item) => (
          <li key={item.id}>
            {item.name} - {item.price}‡ß≥ x {item.quantity} ={" "}
            {item.price * item.quantity}‡ß≥
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
      <h2>Total: {total}‡ß≥</h2>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### Step 1: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Virtual DOM

```javascript
// Memory ‡¶§‡ßá Virtual DOM Tree
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    { type: 'h1', text: 'Shopping Cart' },
    {
      type: 'ul',
      children: [
        { type: 'li', text: '‡¶Ü‡¶Æ - 100‡ß≥ x 2 = 200‡ß≥' },
        { type: 'li', text: '‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ - 50‡ß≥ x 5 = 250‡ß≥' }
      ]
    },
    { type: 'h2', text: 'Total: 450‡ß≥' }
  ]
}
```

### Step 2: User ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ quantity ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã (2 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 3)

```javascript
// State update
setItems((prevItems) =>
  prevItems.map((item) => (item.id === 1 ? { ...item, quantity: 3 } : item))
);
```

### Step 3: ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM

```javascript
// ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM Tree
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    { type: 'h1', text: 'Shopping Cart' },        // Same ‚úì
    {
      type: 'ul',
      children: [
        { type: 'li', text: '‡¶Ü‡¶Æ - 100‡ß≥ x 3 = 300‡ß≥' }, // Changed ‚ö°
        { type: 'li', text: '‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ - 50‡ß≥ x 5 = 250‡ß≥' }   // Same ‚úì
      ]
    },
    { type: 'h2', text: 'Total: 550‡ß≥' }           // Changed ‚ö°
  ]
}
```

### Step 4: React ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶≤

- `h1` ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
- ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ `li` ‚Üí text ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá
- ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º `li` ‚Üí ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
- `h2` ‚Üí text ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá

### Step 5: Real DOM ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ 2‡¶ü‡¶æ update

```javascript
// React ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶á 2‡¶ü‡¶æ operation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá
document.querySelector("li:first-child").textContent = "‡¶Ü‡¶Æ - 100‡ß≥ x 3 = 300‡ß≥";
document.querySelector("h2").textContent = "Total: 550‡ß≥";
```

**‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤:** ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã page reload ‡¶¨‡¶æ re-render ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ 2‡¶ü‡¶æ text update ‡¶π‡¶≤!

---

## ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£

### Example 1: Simple Counter

```javascript
function Counter() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {count}</p>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>+</button>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count - 1)}>-</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º button click ‡¶è:**

1. **State change:** `count` 0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 1 ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º
2. **Virtual DOM comparison:**
   - `div` ‚Üí same
   - `p` text ‚Üí "Count: 0" ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá "Count: 1"
   - ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ `button` ‚Üí same
3. **Real DOM update:** ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `p` element ‡¶è‡¶∞ text update

**Traditional way ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã:**

```javascript
// ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã component ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã
document.innerHTML = `
  <div>
    <p>Count: 1</p>
    <button>+</button>  
    <button>-</button>
  </div>
`;
```

### Example 2: Show/Hide Content

```javascript
function App() {
  const [showContent, setShowContent] = useState(false);

  return (
    <div>
      <button onClick={() => setShowContent(!showContent)}>
        {showContent ? "Hide" : "Show"} Content
      </button>
      {showContent && <p>This is hidden content!</p>}
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Show button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá:**

**Virtual DOM changes:**

```javascript
// Before
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    { type: 'button', text: 'Show Content' }
    // p element ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
  ]
}

// After
{
  type: 'div',
  children: [
    { type: 'button', text: 'Hide Content' },  // text changed
    { type: 'p', text: 'This is hidden content!' }  // new element
  ]
}
```

**Real DOM updates:**

1. Button text update: "Show" ‚Üí "Hide"
2. New p element add

---

## ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® Virtual DOM ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞?

### 1. ‡¶ó‡¶§‡¶ø (Performance)

**Virtual DOM ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ:**

```javascript
// ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø update ‡¶è
document.getElementById("item1").innerHTML = "New text 1"; // Browser recalculate
document.getElementById("item2").innerHTML = "New text 2"; // Browser recalculate
document.getElementById("item3").innerHTML = "New text 3"; // Browser recalculate
// 3 ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ browser calculation!
```

**Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá:**

```javascript
// React ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ changes batch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
// ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶¨ DOM updates ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
// 1 ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ browser calculation!
```

### 2. ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶§‡¶æ (Simplicity)

**Traditional JavaScript:**

```javascript
function updateUI() {
  // ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ DOM manipulation
  const nameEl = document.getElementById("name");
  const emailEl = document.getElementById("email");

  if (user.name) {
    nameEl.style.display = "block";
    nameEl.textContent = user.name;
  } else {
    nameEl.style.display = "none";
  }

  // ... ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï manual work
}
```

**React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá:**

```javascript
function UserProfile({ user }) {
  return (
    <div>
      {user.name && <p>{user.name}</p>}
      {user.email && <p>{user.email}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}
// React automatically ‡¶∏‡¶¨ DOM updates handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá!
```

### 3. Predictability (‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∏)

Virtual DOM ensure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá:

- Same state = Same UI
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® unexpected DOM changes ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á
- UI bugs ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º

---

## ‡¶∏‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶æ

### ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡ßß: Virtual DOM ‡¶ï‡¶ø Real DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§?

**‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:** ‡¶®‡¶æ! Simple applications ‡¶è Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ slow ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ complex applications ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï fast‡•§

**‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®?**

- Simple app: Virtual DOM extra step add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
- Complex app: Virtual DOM ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï unnecessary updates prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá

### ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡ß®: Virtual DOM memory ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ?

**‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:** ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ memory ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ benefits ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ó‡¶£‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

**‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ:**

- Virtual DOM: Lightweight JavaScript objects
- Real DOM: Heavy browser objects
- Trade-off: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø memory vs ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã performance

### ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡ß©: Virtual DOM ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ React ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ?

**‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:** React Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ Virtual DOM ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ React ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡ß™: ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø library ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá Virtual DOM ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá?

**‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:** ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å! Vue.js, Preact ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï modern library ‡¶§‡ßá Virtual DOM ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶® ‡ß´: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø Virtual DOM manually ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø?

**‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞:** ‡¶π‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Å, ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®! ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï complex‡•§ React already optimized Virtual DOM provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Simple example:**

```javascript
// Manual Virtual DOM (educational purpose)
function createElement(tag, props, ...children) {
  return { tag, props, children };
}

// Usage
const virtualElement = createElement(
  "div",
  null,
  createElement("h1", null, "Hello"),
  createElement("p", null, "World")
);
```

---

## ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ

Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø brilliant concept ‡¶Ø‡¶æ modern web development ‡¶è revolution ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

**‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®:**

1. **Virtual DOM = Real DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ JavaScript copy**
2. **‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™:**

   - State change ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º
   - ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Virtual DOM ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º
   - ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá compare ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º
   - ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ changes Real DOM ‡¶è update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º

3. **‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ:**

   - ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ performance
   - ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú development
   - ‡¶ï‡¶Æ bugs

4. **‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ:**
   - Complex applications
   - Frequent UI updates
   - Large component trees

### 1. Prerequisites

React ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá **Node.js** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **npm** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø JavaScript libraries ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø Node.js ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç npm ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá [Node.js ‡¶Ö‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü](https://nodejs.org/en/) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

### 2. Installing Node.js and npm

#### Step 1: Download Node.js

- [Node.js ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü](https://nodejs.org/en/) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **LTS (Long-Term Support)** version ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
- ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞, Terminal ‡¶¨‡¶æ Command Prompt ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```bash
node -v
npm -v
```

### 3. Creating a New React Project

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **Create React App (CRA)** ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶Ü‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Using Create React App (CRA)

**Step 1: Create React App ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ**

Terminal/Command Prompt ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```bash
npx create-react-app my-app
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **my-app** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º dependencies ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Step 2: Project ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ**

```bash

```

### Folder Structure Overview with Real-life Example

React ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®:

#### Example of Folder Structure:

```
my-app/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ node_modules/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ public/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.html
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ favicon.ico
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ src/
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.js
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.css
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.js
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ index.css
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ package.json
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ README.md
```

#### Folder Breakdown:

1. **node_modules/**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ dependencies ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
2. **public/**: public ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **index.html** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá React app ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **src/**: ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá (App.js, index.js, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø)‡•§
4. **package.json**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ dependencies ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scripts ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. package.json Explained

**package.json** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ configuration ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependencies ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

#### Key Sections in package.json:

```json
{
  "name": "my-app",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "private": true,
  "dependencies": {
    "react": "^18.0.0",
    "react-dom": "^18.0.0",
    "react-scripts": "5.0.1"
  },
  "scripts": {
    "start": "react-scripts start",
    "build": "react-scripts build",
    "test": "react-scripts test",
    "eject": "react-scripts eject"
  }
}
```

- **dependencies**: ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ libraries‡•§
- **scripts**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:
  - **npm start**: development server ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - **npm run build**: production build ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - **npm test**: testing ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 5. Example Project: Simple To-Do List

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨‚Äî**Simple To-Do List**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶§ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

#### Step 1: Setting Up the Project

Terminal ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **my-app** ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```bash
npx create-react-app todo-app
cd todo-app
```

---

#### Step 2: Creating the To-Do List Component

**src/App.js** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

function App() {
  const [tasks, setTasks] = useState([]);
  const [newTask, setNewTask] = useState("");

  const handleAddTask = () => {
    setTasks([...tasks, newTask]);
    setNewTask("");
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>To-Do List</h1>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={newTask}
        onChange={(e) => setNewTask(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Add a new task"
      />
      <button onClick={handleAddTask}>Add Task</button>
      <ul>
        {tasks.map((task, index) => (
          <li key={index}>{task}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **useState Hook**: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **useState** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø task list ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® task handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
2. **handleAddTask**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® task list ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç input field ‡¶ü‡¶ø reset ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **map Function**: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **map** function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡¶ø **tasks** array render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Step 3: Adding Interactivity

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® **task** input ‡¶è ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá **Add Task** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶® ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶≤‡ßá task list ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® item ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Step 4: Running and Testing

**npm start** ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®:

```bash
npm start
```

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **http://localhost:3000** ‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ To-Do List ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

### 6. Running the React Project

React ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **npm start** ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø local development server ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ü‡¶ø **http://localhost:3000** ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

### 7. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **Simple To-Do List** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® task ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç task list ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

React environment setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø feature ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® state management ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component rendering‡•§

### 1. Introduction to Vite

**Vite** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø modern frontend build tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ development server ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç build process ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **ESM (ECMAScript Modules)** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Hot Module Replacement (HMR)** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ development environment setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Vite ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ startup time ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç minimal configuration ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã frameworks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Why Use Vite for React?

Vite React ‡¶è‡¶∞ development environment setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Fast Startup**: Traditional bundlers ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Webpack ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º Vite ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ startup time ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Hot Module Replacement (HMR)**: Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ code changes UI ‡¶§‡ßá reflect ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ development process ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì efficient ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
- **Minimal Configuration**: Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ default configuration ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø automatically ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶Ü‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Optimized Build**: Vite production build ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø automatically optimized output ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. Installing React with Vite

Vite ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá React setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá step-by-step ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### Step 1: Installing Vite

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá, **npm** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **yarn** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Vite ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Terminal ‡¶¨‡¶æ Command Prompt ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ command ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```bash
npm create vite@latest my-react-app
```

‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ

```bash
yarn create vite my-react-app
```

**my-react-app** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã project ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

#### Step 2: Setting Up the React Project

Vite ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, Vite ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ options ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø **React** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **JavaScript** (‡¶¨‡¶æ TypeScript) select ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

```bash
cd my-react-app
npm install
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, **cd my-react-app** command ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá project ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **npm install** command ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá dependencies install ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

#### Step 3: Running the Development Server

Development server ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ command ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®:

```bash
npm run dev
```

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ local server ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç browser ‡¶è application preview ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ HMR feature ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, code ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßá reflect ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

Output:

```
VITE vX.X.X  ready in 300 ms

  ‚ûú  Local:   http://localhost:3000/
  ‚ûú  Network: use --host to expose
```

‡¶è‡¶á URL ‡¶è ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ React application ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

### 4. Folder Structure Overview

Vite ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá React setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® folder structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```
my-react-app
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ node_modules
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ public
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ src
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ App.jsx
‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ main.jsx
‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ index.css
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ .gitignore
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ index.html
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ package.json
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ vite.config.js
```

- **node_modules**: React ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Other 3rd Party tools ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á Folder ‡¶è Touch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§
- **public**: ‡¶è‡¶á Folder ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Website ‡¶è‡¶∞ Public Assets ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Images, Files, Videos etc ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- **src**: ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ **App.jsx** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **main.jsx** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ React components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç entry point‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ React Application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø 95% ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á Folder ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **public**: Static files ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **index.html**: Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® HTML ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá `<div id="root"></div>` root ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá div element ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Application ‡¶è‡¶∞ Container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶¨ React Code ‡¶è‡¶á root ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶á render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- **vite.config.js**: Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ configuration ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ì Touch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

---

## Explanation of main.jsx File

### Table of Contents

### 1. Code Overview

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React Application ‡¶è‡¶∞ Entry Point ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `React` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `ReactDOM` ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Application-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

### 2. What is StrictMode?

`StrictMode` ‡¶π‡¶≤ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Deprecated API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ Side-Effect ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ Development Mode-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, Production Mode-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `StrictMode` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø Application-‡¶ï‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá Development Console-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü:

```jsx
<StrictMode>
  <App />
</StrictMode>
```

### 3. How does createRoot Work?

`createRoot` ‡¶π‡¶≤ `React 18` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® API, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React Application-‡¶ï‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ReactDOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Method ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã `ReactDOM.render` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(
  <StrictMode>
    <App />
  </StrictMode>
);
```

- `createRoot` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML ‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á Element ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ `id` `'root'`‡•§
- ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `render` Method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `<App />` Component-‡¶ü‡¶ø `StrictMode` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã Application ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ê `root` Div-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá Render ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

### 4. Rendering Process with ReactDOM

‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `ReactDOM.render` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶Æ, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ `React 18` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `ReactDOM.createRoot` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `.render()` Method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Rendering Performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Feature ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Concurrent Mode ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Discussion on File Imports

```javascript
import { StrictMode } from "react";
import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
import "./index.css";
import App from "./App.jsx";
```

- **`StrictMode`**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `react` ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- **`createRoot`**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `react-dom/client` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- **`'./index.css'`**: Stylesheet Import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Application ‡¶è‡¶∞ Style ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **`App`**: `'./App.jsx'` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ Application Component Import ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ React Application-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá Render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 5. Real-life Example Project

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple React component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá "Hello, Vite!" ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Example Code:

**App.jsx**

```jsx
function App() {
  return (
    <div className="App">
      <h1>Hello, Vite!</h1>
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**main.jsx**

```jsx
import React from "react";
import ReactDOM from "react-dom";
import App from "./App";
import "./index.css";

ReactDOM.createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <App />
  </React.StrictMode>
);
```

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° Vite environment ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø browser ‡¶è "Hello, Vite!" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

Vite ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá React setup ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø traditional bundlers ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç minimal configuration ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ modern React development ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡•§ Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ development environment ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

Vite ‡¶è‡¶∞ speed ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexibility React ‡¶è‡¶∞ modern development environment ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ‡•§

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-04: React Render HTML

### Table of Contents:

1. [What Does Rendering HTML Mean in React?](#what-does-rendering-html-mean-in-react)

### 1. What Does Rendering HTML Mean in React?

**Rendering HTML** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã HTML elements ‡¶¨‡¶æ components-‡¶ï‡ßá web browser ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ traditional JavaScript ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá DOM (Document Object Model) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `document.createElement()` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `innerHTML` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá HTML dynamically generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ **React** ‡¶è, rendering process ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì streamlined ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø HTML code **JSX (JavaScript XML)** syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá efficiently render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã user interface ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á UI ‡¶ï‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ real DOM ‡¶è reflect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **ReactDOM** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ web page ‡¶è HTML render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. How React Renders HTML

#### JSX Syntax

**JSX (JavaScript XML)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶∞ special syntax ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá embedded ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ JSX ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã structure ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá React component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá rendering ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of JSX:

```jsx
const element = <h1>Hello, world!</h1>;
```

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá **JSX**‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶á JSX ‡¶ï‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM ‡¶è render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### ReactDOM.render()

**ReactDOM.render()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá React component ‡¶¨‡¶æ JSX ‡¶ï‡ßá real DOM ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Syntax:

```jsx
ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

‡¶è‡¶á example ‡¶è, **element** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML ‡¶¨‡¶æ React component ‡¶ü‡¶ø render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **'root'** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ id, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á content inject ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
import React from "react";
import ReactDOM from "react-dom";

const element = <h1>Hello, React!</h1>;

ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø **index.html** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **div** element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ id ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá "root":

```html
<div id="root"></div>
```

---

### 3. Rendering Dynamic Content

React ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ static HTML ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç dynamic content render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, user input ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ data dynamically update ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Rendering Dynamic Content:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import ReactDOM from "react-dom";

function App() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("React");

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Hello, {name}!</h1>
      <input
        type="text"
        value={name}
        onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

ReactDOM.render(<App />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Explanation:

1. **useState Hook**: ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ **useState** hook ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **name** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶ø‡•§
2. **Dynamic Rendering**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® user input field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á **name** value dynamically update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá rendering ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Real-life Example of Rendering HTML

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø e-commerce website ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® product ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á product ‡¶ü‡¶ø dynamically render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import ReactDOM from "react-dom";

function ProductList() {
  const [products, setProducts] = useState(["Product 1", "Product 2"]);

  const addProduct = () => {
    setProducts([...products, `Product ${products.length + 1}`]);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h1>Product List</h1>
      <ul>
        {products.map((product, index) => (
          <li key={index}>{product}</li>
        ))}
      </ul>
      <button onClick={addProduct}>Add Product</button>
    </div>
  );
}

ReactDOM.render(<ProductList />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Explanation:

1. **useState**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **products** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø array ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® product ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ **addProduct** function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **products** ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Dynamic Rendering**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® product ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, **ProductList** component ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç updated product list ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 5. React Virtual DOM and Rendering Efficiency

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ HTML rendering ‡¶è‡¶§ efficient ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM**‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø React component ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, React ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã DOM ‡¶ï‡ßá re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá Virtual DOM ‡¶è changes apply ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ minimal changes real DOM ‡¶è implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá unnecessary re-rendering ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá HTML rendering process ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **JSX** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **ReactDOM** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ static content ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, dynamic content ‡¶ì ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá UI ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç smooth ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, React modern web applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø essential tool ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶†‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI rendering ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 1. What is JSX?

**JSX (JavaScript XML)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø syntax extension, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã structure ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì JSX ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **JavaScript** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ syntax ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **React** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá JSX ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø JSX ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§

##### Example of JSX:

```jsx
const element = <h1>Hello, World!</h1>;
```

‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá **<h1>Hello, World!</h1>** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ‡¶§‡ßá JavaScript ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá DOM ‡¶è render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 2. Why JSX is Important

JSX React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **JavaScript** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá **UI components** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Readable and Declarative**: JSX HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø readable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç declarative ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ development experience ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Integration with JavaScript**: JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á JavaScript expressions ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logic UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá integrate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Faster Rendering**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Virtual DOM** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá JSX ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ HTML render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. JSX Syntax

JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ syntax ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functionality ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡•§

#### Embedding Expressions in JSX

JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **JavaScript expressions** embed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã value JSX ‡¶è curly braces `{}` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Embedding JavaScript in JSX:

```jsx
const name = "React";
const element = <h1>Hello, {name}!</h1>;
```

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, **name** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï JavaScript variable ‡¶ü‡¶ø JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá DOM ‡¶è **"Hello, React!"** render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### JSX Elements and Components

JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ HTML elements ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç React components ‡¶ï‡ßá JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of JSX with Components:

```jsx
function Welcome(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}

const element = <Welcome name="React" />;
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **Welcome** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ **props** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamic data render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. JSX vs HTML

‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì JSX HTML ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **class vs className**: HTML ‡¶è **class** attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ JSX ‡¶è **className** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ **class** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ reserved keyword‡•§

   ```jsx
   <div className="container"></div>
   ```

2. **Self-closing Tags**: JSX ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø tag self-close ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã closing tag ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

   ```jsx
   <img src="image.jpg" alt="Sample" />
   ```

3. **JSX attributes in camelCase**: HTML attributes, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **onclick** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **onchange** JSX ‡¶è camelCase ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

   ```jsx
   <button onClick={handleClick}>Click Me</button>
   ```

---

### 5. Real-life Example of JSX

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **User Profile** component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user's name, email, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç profile picture ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
function UserProfile(props) {
  return (
    <div className="profile-card">
      <img src={props.avatar} alt="User Avatar" />
      <h2>{props.name}</h2>
      <p>Email: {props.email}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

const element = (
  <UserProfile
    avatar="https://example.com/avatar.jpg"
    name="John Doe"
    email="john.doe@example.com"
  />
);

ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Explanation:

1. **UserProfile Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **UserProfile** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ **name**, **email**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **avatar** image ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Props Usage**: **props.name**, **props.email** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá component dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Rendering**: ReactDOM.render() method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶ï‡ßá DOM ‡¶è render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Common JSX Mistakes and Best Practices

#### Mistake 1: Forgetting to Close Tags

JSX ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element self-closing ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã child ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™:

```jsx
// Incorrect
<input>

// Correct
<input />
```

#### Mistake 2: Returning Multiple Elements Without Wrapping

JSX ‡¶è multiple elements return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø parent element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™:

```jsx
// Incorrect
return (
  <h1>Hello</h1>
  <p>World</p>
);

// Correct
return (
  <div>
    <h1>Hello</h1>
    <p>World</p>
  </div>
);
```

---

### 7. Conclusion

**JSX** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® syntax ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JavaScript ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá HTML elements ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø declarative ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable syntax ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá UI development ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ static content ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, dynamic JavaScript expressions ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ core concepts ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç complex UI ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
