### 1. What are React Components?

**React components** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ building blocks, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø React component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript function ‡¶¨‡¶æ class ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **HTML-like** structure (JSX) return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Components independent ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of a Simple React Component:

```jsx
function Welcome() {
  return <h1>Hello, React!</h1>;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, **Welcome** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React function component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **Hello, React!** text ‡¶ï‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø complex UI ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü reusable ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

---

### 2. Types of React Components

React ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ component ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá: **Function Components** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Class Components**‡•§

#### Function Components

**Function Components** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã JavaScript functions ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JSX return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã React Hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Function components ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lightweight ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Function Component:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}
```

#### Class Components

**Class Components** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ES6 ‡¶è‡¶∞ JavaScript classes ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React.Component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods support ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá function components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of Class Component:

```jsx
class Welcome extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}
```

---

### 3. Props in React Components

**Props** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component ‡¶è‡¶∞ external data ‡¶Ø‡¶æ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø immutable, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá props modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã dynamic data ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of Passing Props:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}

const element = <Greeting name="John" />;
ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá, **name** prop parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **Greeting** component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI ‡¶§‡ßá dynamic data ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. State in React Components

**State** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component ‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶ï‡ßá dynamically ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Function components ‡¶è state handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **useState Hook** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç class components ‡¶è **this.state** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ State dynamic data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of State in Function Component:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Counter() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div>
      <p>You clicked {count} times</p>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>Click me</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

##### Example of State in Class Component:

```jsx
class Counter extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { count: 0 };
  }

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <p>You clicked {this.state.count} times</p>
        <button onClick={() => this.setState({ count: this.state.count + 1 })}>
          Click me
        </button>
      </div>
    );
  }
}
```

---

### 5. Lifecycle Methods in Class Components

React class components ‡¶è **lifecycle methods** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá (mounting, updating, unmounting) ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ lifecycle methods ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **componentDidMount**: component render ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **componentDidUpdate**: component re-render ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **componentWillUnmount**: component destroy ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of componentDidMount:

```jsx
class Timer extends React.Component {
  componentDidMount() {
    this.timerID = setInterval(() => this.tick(), 1000);
  }

  tick() {
    console.log("Timer is ticking");
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Timer Running</h1>;
  }
}
```

---

### 6. Real-life Example of React Components

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **User Profile** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ, ‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç address ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
function UserProfile(props) {
  return (
    <div className="profile">
      <h2>{props.name}</h2>
      <p>Age: {props.age}</p>
      <p>Address: {props.address}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

const element = (
  <UserProfile name="John Doe" age="30" address="123 React Street" />
);

ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Explanation:

- **UserProfile Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reusable React component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá dynamic data render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- **Props**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ **name**, **age**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **address** props ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá **UserProfile** component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **components** modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ cornerstone, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü, reusable ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React components ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® props, state, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá complex UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Function components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç hooks ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ lifecycle methods ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-07: React Class Components

### Table of Contents:

1. [What is a React Class Component?](#what-is-a-react-class-component)

---

### 1. What is a React Class Component?

**React Class Components** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã traditional React components ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ES6 ‡¶è‡¶∞ JavaScript class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Class components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state management, lifecycle methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç complex functionality ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì function components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React Hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ì class components ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ complex scenarios ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Class components React.Component class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á **render()** method ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ JSX ‡¶¨‡¶æ React elements return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Defining a React Class Component

React class component define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ES6 class ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **React.Component** class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

##### Example of Class Component:

```jsx
import React, { Component } from "react";

class Welcome extends Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}

export default Welcome;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **Welcome Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **Welcome** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React class component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **React.Component** ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **render() Method**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï React class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **render()** method ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá JSX ‡¶¨‡¶æ React elements return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. **props**: Class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **props** **this.props** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. React Class vs Function Components

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßá class components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ function components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React Hooks ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá function components ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### Function Components:

- **Simpler**: Function components ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lightweight‡•§
- **Hooks**: React Hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá function components state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Less Boilerplate**: Function components ‡¶è class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã boilerplate ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

#### Class Components:

- **State and Lifecycle**: Class components ‡¶è state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- **Legacy Code**: ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã React ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì class components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Complex Features**: ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ complex feature class components ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. State in Class Components

**State** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è‡¶∞ UI ‡¶ï‡ßá update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Class components ‡¶è **this.state** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **this.setState()** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of State in Class Component:

```jsx
import React, { Component } from "react";

class Counter extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { count: 0 };
  }

  increment = () => {
    this.setState({ count: this.state.count + 1 });
  };

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <p>Count: {this.state.count}</p>
        <button onClick={this.increment}>Increment</button>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

export default Counter;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **this.state**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **count** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **this.setState()**: state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **this.setState()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **render()**: state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç updated data UI ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 5. Lifecycle Methods in Class Components

React class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ feature ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **lifecycle methods**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á methods component ‡¶è‡¶∞ lifecycle ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá (mounting, updating, unmounting) execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Common Lifecycle Methods:

1. **componentDidMount**: Component render ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **componentDidUpdate**: Component re-render ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **componentWillUnmount**: Component destroy ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Lifecycle Method:

```jsx
import React, { Component } from "react";

class Timer extends Component {
  componentDidMount() {
    this.timerID = setInterval(() => this.tick(), 1000);
  }

  componentWillUnmount() {
    clearInterval(this.timerID);
  }

  tick() {
    console.log("Timer ticking");
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Timer is running</h1>;
  }
}

export default Timer;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **componentDidMount**: Timer ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **setInterval** ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component render ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **componentWillUnmount**: Component destroy ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá **clearInterval** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá timer ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Props in Class Components

**Props** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã external data ‡¶Ø‡¶æ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá class component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Class components ‡¶è props **this.props** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Props in Class Component:

```jsx
import React, { Component } from "react";

class Welcome extends Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Welcome, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}

export default Welcome;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **this.props**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **name** prop pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **this.props.name** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Real-life Example of React Class Components

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **User Profile** class component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏ dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
import React, { Component } from "react";

class UserProfile extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { age: 25 };
  }

  incrementAge = () => {
    this.setState({ age: this.state.age + 1 });
  };

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <h2>{this.props.name}</h2>
        <p>Age: {this.state.age}</p>
        <button onClick={this.incrementAge}>Increase Age</button>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

export default UserProfile;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **UserProfile Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **UserProfile** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Props and State**: User ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ **props** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏ **state** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Increment Function**: **this.setState()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

React class components modern web development ‡¶è‡¶∞ cornerstone, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state management ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì function components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React Hooks ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ì ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç complex applications ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶ì ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ Class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá React ‡¶è‡¶∞ powerful features ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® state, props, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

# Chapter-07.1: Lifecycle Methods in Class Components

### Table of Contents:

1. [What are Lifecycle Methods?](#what-are-lifecycle-methods)

   - [Mounting Phase](#mounting-phase)
   - [Updating Phase](#updating-phase)
   - [Unmounting Phase](#unmounting-phase)
4. [Real-life Example of Lifecycle Methods](#real-life-example-of-lifecycle-methods)
5. [Best Practices for Using Lifecycle Methods](#best-practices-for-using-lifecycle-methods)
6. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

---

### 1. What are Lifecycle Methods?

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ class components ‡¶è **lifecycle methods** ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ method, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ initialization ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá update ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç destruction ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á methods ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **Lifecycle methods** component render, update, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unmount ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: data fetching, DOM manipulation, cleanup, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

### 2. Phases of Component Lifecycle

React component ‡¶è‡¶∞ lifecycle ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§:

1. **Mounting**: Component DOM ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Updating**: Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ props ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **Unmounting**: Component ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Lifecycle Methods in Each Phase

#### Mounting Phase

Mounting phase ‡¶è component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç DOM ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ lifecycle methods ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã sequentially call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

1. **constructor()**
2. **getDerivedStateFromProps()**
3. **render()**
4. **componentDidMount()**

##### Explanation of Each Method:

- **constructor(props)**: Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ initial state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø constructor method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø lifecycle ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ method ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **this.state** initialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

  ```javascript
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { count: 0 };
  }
  ```

- **getDerivedStateFromProps(props, state)**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø static method ‡¶Ø‡¶æ props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  static getDerivedStateFromProps(props, state) {
    if (props.reset) {
      return { count: 0 };
    }
    return null;
  }
  ```

- **render()**: render() method component ‡¶è‡¶∞ UI define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JSX return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø mandatory method ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø re-rendering trigger ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  render() {
    return <h1>Count: {this.state.count}</h1>;
  }
  ```

- **componentDidMount()**: component ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ render ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá **componentDidMount** execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø API call ‡¶¨‡¶æ DOM manipulation ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡•§

  ```javascript
  componentDidMount() {
    console.log("Component mounted!");
  }
  ```

---

#### Updating Phase

Updating phase ‡¶è component ‡¶è‡¶∞ props ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá sequentially ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ lifecycle methods ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

1. **getDerivedStateFromProps()**
2. **shouldComponentUpdate()**
3. **render()**
4. **getSnapshotBeforeUpdate()**
5. **componentDidUpdate()**

##### Explanation of Each Method:

- **shouldComponentUpdate(nextProps, nextState)**: ‡¶è‡¶á method return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá true ‡¶¨‡¶æ false, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component re-render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø performance optimization ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡•§

  ```javascript
  shouldComponentUpdate(nextProps, nextState) {
    return nextState.count !== this.state.count;
  }
  ```

- **getSnapshotBeforeUpdate(prevProps, prevState)**: DOM update ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶∞ snapshot ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø scrolling position, DOM updates track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  getSnapshotBeforeUpdate(prevProps, prevState) {
    if (prevState.count < this.state.count) {
      return "Count increased";
    }
    return null;
  }
  ```

- **componentDidUpdate(prevProps, prevState, snapshot)**: Component update ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **getSnapshotBeforeUpdate** ‡¶è‡¶∞ return value receive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

  ```javascript
  componentDidUpdate(prevProps, prevState, snapshot) {
    if (snapshot) {
      console.log(snapshot);
    }
  }
  ```

---

#### Unmounting Phase

Unmounting phase ‡¶è component ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶è‡¶á method ‡¶ü‡¶ø call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

- **componentWillUnmount()**: Component unmount ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á method execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø cleanup ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: timers, subscriptions, event listeners remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

  ```javascript
  componentWillUnmount() {
    console.log("Component will unmount!");
  }
  ```

---

### 4. Real-life Example of Lifecycle Methods

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Timer** component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá update ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component unmount ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá timer ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
import React, { Component } from "react";

class Timer extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { seconds: 0 };
  }

  componentDidMount() {
    this.timerID = setInterval(() => {
      this.setState((prevState) => ({ seconds: prevState.seconds + 1 }));
    }, 1000);
  }

  componentDidUpdate() {
    console.log("Timer updated:", this.state.seconds);
  }

  componentWillUnmount() {
    clearInterval(this.timerID);
    console.log("Timer cleared");
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Seconds: {this.state.seconds}</h1>;
  }
}

export default Timer;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **componentDidMount**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá interval set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç timer ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá update ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **componentDidUpdate**: Timer ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø update console ‡¶è log ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **componentWillUnmount**: Component unmount ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá interval clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. Best Practices for Using Lifecycle Methods

1. **Avoid Excessive use of componentDidUpdate**: Unnecessary re-renders ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **componentDidUpdate** ‡¶è conditionals ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
2. **Perform Cleanup in componentWillUnmount**: Memory leak ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá cleanup ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
3. **Avoid Direct DOM Manipulation**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ built-in state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM access ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ class components ‡¶è **lifecycle methods** component ‡¶è‡¶∞ initialization, update, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç destruction phases ‡¶ï‡ßá manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Proper use of these lifecycle methods allows developers to control the behavior of components effectively, manage resources, and optimize performance, making React applications more robust and efficient.

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-07.2: Props in Class Components

### Table of Contents:

1. [What are Props?](#what-are-props)
2. [Why Use Props in Class Components?](#why-use-props-in-class-components)
3. [How to Access Props in Class Components](#how-to-access-props-in-class-components)
4. [Passing Props to Class Components](#passing-props-to-class-components)
5. [Default Props](#default-props)
6. [Prop Types for Validation](#prop-types-for-validation)
7. [Real-life Example of Props Usage](#real-life-example-of-props-usage)
8. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

---

### 1. What are Props?

**Props** ‡¶¨‡¶æ "properties" ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è data passing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Props ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã immutable, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, child component ‡¶è props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamic content ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Why Use Props in Class Components?

Props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

- Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data child component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Component ‡¶ï‡ßá configurable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ reusability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. How to Access Props in Class Components

Class components ‡¶è props access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `this.props` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
class Greeting extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}
```

**Explanation**:

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **this.props.name** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá props ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã `name` property access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Passing Props to Class Components

Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è props ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component attribute ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
class App extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return <Greeting name="John" age={25} />;
  }
}

class Greeting extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>
        <p>Your age is {this.props.age}.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(<App />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

**Explanation**:

- **name** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **age** props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá **Greeting** component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **this.props.name** ‡¶ì **this.props.age** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

**Output**:

```
Hello, John!
Your age is 25.
```

---

### 5. Default Props

React ‡¶è **default props** ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è props ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá default value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
class Greeting extends React.Component {
  static defaultProps = {
    name: "Guest",
  };

  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(<Greeting />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

**Explanation**:

- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **name** prop ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßá default value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá "Guest" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

**Output**:

```
Hello, Guest!
```

---

### 6. Prop Types for Validation

React ‡¶è prop types ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá props validation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ data component ‡¶è pass ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
import PropTypes from "prop-types";

class Greeting extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}

Greeting.propTypes = {
  name: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
};

ReactDOM.render(<Greeting name="John" />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

**Explanation**:

- **PropTypes** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá props ‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **name** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø string ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§

---

### 7. Real-life Example of Props Usage

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple profile component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```javascript
class Profile extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Name: {this.props.name}</h1>
        <p>Profession: {this.props.profession}</p>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

class App extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <Profile name="Alice" profession="Engineer" />
        <Profile name="Bob" profession="Designer" />
      </div>
    );
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(<App />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

**Explanation**:

- **App** component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **Profile** component ‡¶è **name** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **profession** props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø **Profile** component ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

**Output**:

```
Name: Alice
Profession: Engineer

Name: Bob
Profession: Designer
```

---

### 8. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ class components ‡¶è **props** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá data ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ parent component dynamic data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **Default props** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **prop types validation** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá props ‡¶è‡¶∞ type ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

# Chapter-08: Props in Functional Components

### Table of Contents:

1. [What are Props in React?](#what-are-props-in-react)
2. [Why are Props Important?](#why-are-props-important)
3. [How to Pass Props in React](#how-to-pass-props-in-react)
4. [Accessing Props in Components](#accessing-props-in-components)
5. [Default Props](#default-props)
6. [Props vs State](#props-vs-state)
7. [Real-life Example of Props](#real-life-example-of-props)
8. [Conclusion](#conclusion)

---

### 1. What are Props in React?

**Props** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React components ‡¶è‡¶∞ external data ‡¶Ø‡¶æ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **props** system component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data share ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamic UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **Props** immutable, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá props ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ read-only data ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

Props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá React components reusability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Props:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **props.name** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **name** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï external data component ‡¶è dynamically ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Why are Props Important?

Props React ‡¶è **reusable** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **dynamic** component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã parent-child component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data communication ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá props pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá, child component ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á props data ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamic content ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Key Reasons Props are Important:

- **Reusability**: Props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® data ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Dynamic Rendering**: Props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá dynamic data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ action ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Unidirectional Data Flow**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ props system parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è data flow ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. How to Pass Props in React

React component ‡¶è props pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá JSX attributes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã syntax ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è props pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of Passing Props:

```jsx
function Welcome(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}

const element = <Welcome name="John" />;
ReactDOM.render(element, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Explanation:

1. **Parent Component**: Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá **name="John"** props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Child Component**: Child component (Welcome) **props.name** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. Accessing Props in Components

**Props** ‡¶ï‡ßá class component ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function component ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã component ‡¶è props access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡•§

#### Accessing Props in Function Components:

Function components ‡¶è **props** function ‡¶è‡¶∞ argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Welcome(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}
```

#### Accessing Props in Class Components:

Class components ‡¶è **this.props** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá props access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
class Welcome extends React.Component {
  render() {
    return <h1>Hello, {this.props.name}!</h1>;
  }
}
```

---

### 5. Default Props

‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá, component ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã props pass ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá default value set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **defaultProps** feature ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Default Props:

```jsx
function Welcome(props) {
  return <h1>Hello, {props.name}!</h1>;
}

Welcome.defaultProps = {
  name: "Guest",
};
```

#### Explanation:

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **name** props pass ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá, **'Guest'** default ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Props vs State

**Props** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **State** ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á component ‡¶è‡¶∞ data manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| **Props**                      | **State**                              |
| ------------------------------ | -------------------------------------- |
| Immutable                      | Mutable                                |
| Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá pass ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º | Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º     |
| Read-only                      | Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º |
| Unidirectional data flow ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá   | Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá       |

#### Key Differences:

- **Props** parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **State** component ‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Real-life Example of Props

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Product Card** component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá product ‡¶è‡¶∞ image, ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á data child component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Example:

```jsx
function ProductCard(props) {
  return (
    <div className="product-card">
      <img src={props.image} alt={props.name} />
      <h2>{props.name}</h2>
      <p>Price: ${props.price}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

const product = {
  name: "Laptop",
  price: 1200,
  image: "https://example.com/laptop.jpg",
};

ReactDOM.render(
  <ProductCard
    name={product.name}
    price={product.price}
    image={product.image}
  />,
  document.getElementById("root")
);
```

#### Explanation:

1. **ProductCard Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **ProductCard** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **name**, **price**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **image** pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Parent Component**: Parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá product ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ data props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá **ProductCard** component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Rendering**: Product ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ, ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Props** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data flow ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç communication ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Props immutable ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ predictable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç stable component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

Props ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 1. What is State in React Class Components?

**State** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç appearance ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø dynamically manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Class components ‡¶è **state** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá UI ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ State ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø JavaScript object ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è‡¶∞ data ‡¶¨‡¶æ UI control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of State:

```jsx
class Counter extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { count: 0 };
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Count: {this.state.count}</h1>;
  }
}
```

---

### 2. What is Lifecycle in React Class Components?

**Component lifecycle** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ creation ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá destruction ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React class component ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá:

1. **Mounting**: Component DOM ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ insert ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Updating**: Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ props ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **Unmounting**: Component DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ lifecycle methods ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á methods component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® component ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ destroy ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Managing State in Class Components

#### Setting Initial State

Class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ **constructor()** method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá initial state set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **this.state** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá state ‡¶è‡¶∞ initial value ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example of Initial State:

```jsx
class Greeting extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { message: "Hello, World!" };
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>{this.state.message}</h1>;
  }
}
```

#### Updating State with setState

State ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá **this.setState()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø asynchronous ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ component re-render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example of Updating State:

```jsx
class Counter extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { count: 0 };
  }

  increment = () => {
    this.setState({ count: this.state.count + 1 });
  };

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Count: {this.state.count}</h1>
        <button onClick={this.increment}>Increment</button>
      </div>
    );
  }
}
```

#### Explanation:

1. **this.state**: Initial state set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **this.state** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **this.setState()**: state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **this.setState()** method ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç count increment ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. React Class Component Lifecycle Phases

React class component lifecycle ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§:

#### Mounting Phase

‡¶è‡¶á phase ‡¶è component DOM ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ insert ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common lifecycle methods ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **constructor()**
- **componentDidMount()**

#### Updating Phase

Component ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¨‡¶æ props ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá component update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á phase ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common lifecycle methods ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **shouldComponentUpdate()**
- **componentDidUpdate()**

#### Unmounting Phase

Component ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá remove ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶á phase ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø common lifecycle method ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **componentWillUnmount()**

---

### 5. Common Lifecycle Methods

#### componentDidMount

**componentDidMount** lifecycle method ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® component DOM ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ API calls ‡¶¨‡¶æ external resources load ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
class Timer extends React.Component {
  componentDidMount() {
    this.timerID = setInterval(() => this.tick(), 1000);
  }

  tick() {
    console.log("Timer is running");
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Timer Started</h1>;
  }
}
```

#### componentDidUpdate

**componentDidUpdate** method ‡¶ü‡¶ø component update ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø props ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
class Counter extends React.Component {
  componentDidUpdate(prevProps, prevState) {
    if (this.state.count !== prevState.count) {
      console.log("Count updated");
    }
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Updated Count: {this.state.count}</h1>;
  }
}
```

#### componentWillUnmount

**componentWillUnmount** method component destroy ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ resources (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® timers, subscriptions) clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
class Timer extends React.Component {
  componentWillUnmount() {
    clearInterval(this.timerID);
  }

  render() {
    return <h1>Timer Stopped</h1>;
  }
}
```

---

### 6. Real-life Example: Timer with State and Lifecycle

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø timer component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá timer increment ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component destroy ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá timer ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
class Timer extends React.Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props);
    this.state = { seconds: 0 };
  }

  componentDidMount() {
    this.timerID = setInterval(() => this.tick(), 1000);
  }

  componentWillUnmount() {
    clearInterval(this.timerID);
  }

  tick() {
    this.setState({ seconds: this.state.seconds + 1 });
  }

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Timer: {this.state.seconds} seconds</h1>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

export default Timer;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **State Management**: Timer component ‡¶è‡¶∞ state initial value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá 0 set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Lifecycle Methods**: **componentDidMount** method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá timer ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **componentWillUnmount** method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá timer clear ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **State Update**: **this.setState()** method ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡ßá state update ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç seconds value ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 7. Conclusion

React class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ **state** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **lifecycle methods** React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶Æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® features, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ **State** component ‡¶è‡¶∞ internal data manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **lifecycle methods** component ‡¶è‡¶∞ lifecycle ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

State ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø complex functionality handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® asynchronous operations (API calls), timers, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç resource management‡•§ Class components ‡¶è state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component behavior ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç rendering process ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful tool React developers ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-9.1: React State in Functional Components

## You will learn:

1. useState ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º
2. useState ‡¶π‡ßÅ‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá
3. ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï state ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü

## State: A Component's Memory

- React ‡¶è State ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø to-do list ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ State ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶®‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

State ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ action ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ State ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ static ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã user interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ State ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶≤-‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user experience ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã interaction ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ input field ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, image carousel-‡¶è "next" ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, "buy" ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ü‡¶ø shopping cart ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∑‡¶Ø‡¶º "‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá" ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® input value, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® image, shopping cart‡•§ React ‡¶è, ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßá state ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

- ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‚Äúnext‚Äù ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‚Äúbuy‚Äù ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∏ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶¨‡¶ø, ‡¶∂‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü‡•§ **React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßá state ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§**

## ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º

### 1. What are Events in React?

**Events** React ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, input field ‡¶è ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, form submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶á events‡•§ React events web browsers ‡¶è‡¶∞ native DOM events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ React events **camelCase** ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inline **JavaScript functions** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **function references** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 2. How Events Work in React

React ‡¶è event handling ‡¶è‡¶∞ process ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡•§ Traditional DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ events ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `onclick`, `onchange` ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã lowercase ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ React ‡¶è event attributes ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **camelCase** ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `onClick`, `onChange` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§ React events **synthetic events** ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ native browser events ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

Synthetic events cross-browser compatibility ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ Virtual DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá efficiently ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. Handling Events in React

React ‡¶è events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá inline function ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ function reference ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React event handling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

##### Example of Event Handling:

```jsx
function ButtonClick() {
  const handleClick = () => {
    alert("Button was clicked!");
  };

  return <button onClick={handleClick}>Click Me</button>;
}
```

#### Explanation:

- **handleClick function**: ‡¶è‡¶á function ‡¶ü‡¶ø button ‡¶è click ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **onClick event**: **onClick** event attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá **handleClick** function button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 4. Event Handling in Functional and Class Components

React ‡¶è event handling class components ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functional components ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Functional components ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø function declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá class components ‡¶è event handlers typically class methods ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Event Handling in Functional Components:

```jsx
function Greeting() {
  const handleClick = () => {
    console.log("Hello!");
  };

  return <button onClick={handleClick}>Greet</button>;
}
```

#### Event Handling in Class Components:

```jsx
class Greeting extends React.Component {
  handleClick = () => {
    console.log("Hello!");
  };

  render() {
    return <button onClick={this.handleClick}>Greet</button>;
  }
}
```

#### Key Differences:

- **Functional Components**: ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø function declaration ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Class Components**: **this** keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá class methods ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá events handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 5. Passing Arguments to Event Handlers

React ‡¶è event handlers ‡¶è arguments pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ events automatically **event object** ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø custom arguments pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá inline function ‡¶¨‡¶æ arrow function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§

##### Example of Passing Arguments:

```jsx
function ButtonClick() {
  const handleClick = (message) => {
    alert(message);
  };

  return (
    <button onClick={() => handleClick("Button was clicked!")}>Click Me</button>
  );
}
```

#### Explanation:

- **Arrow Function**: Inline arrow function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá custom message pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 6. Common React Event Types

React ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ events ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® element ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common event types ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### Click Events

Click event ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø event ‡¶Ø‡¶æ button, link, ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã clickable element ‡¶è ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
<button onClick={() => alert("Button clicked!")}>Click Me</button>
```

#### Form Events

Form elements ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **input**, **select**, **textarea** ‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá **onChange**, **onSubmit** events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Form() {
  const handleChange = (event) => {
    console.log(event.target.value);
  };

  return <input type="text" onChange={handleChange} placeholder="Type here" />;
}
```

#### Keyboard Events

Keyboard events ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá keyboard interaction handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® key press ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function KeyPress() {
  const handleKeyPress = (event) => {
    console.log(`Key pressed: ${event.key}`);
  };

  return <input type="text" onKeyPress={handleKeyPress} />;
}
```

---

### 7. Real-life Example: Form Handling with Events

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï, ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple form ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç email input field ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç submit button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá form data handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

function SimpleForm() {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ name: "", email: "" });

  const handleChange = (event) => {
    const { name, value } = event.target;
    setFormData((prevData) => ({
      ...prevData,
      [name]: value,
    }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    console.log("Form Submitted: ", formData);
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <div>
        <label>Name:</label>
        <input
          type="text"
          name="name"
          value={formData.name}
          onChange={handleChange}
        />
      </div>
      <div>
        <label>Email:</label>
        <input
          type="email"
          name="email"
          value={formData.email}
          onChange={handleChange}
        />
      </div>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default SimpleForm;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **useState Hook**: **useState** hook ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ **name** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **email** state management ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **handleChange function**: Input field ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á data **handleChange** function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá state ‡¶è store ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **handleSubmit function**: Form submit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º **handleSubmit** function prevent ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá browser ‡¶è‡¶∞ default behavior ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data console ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 8. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ developer ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç interactive user interfaces ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **synthetic events** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® incompatibility ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø unified event handling system ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ actions ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **button click**, **keyboard input**, **form submission** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **functional components** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **class components** ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ **Props** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã dynamic ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **state management** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü handling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã **camelCase** ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inline function ‡¶¨‡¶æ reference ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Cross-browser compatibility ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç performance ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶á‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá, interactive ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive web applications ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 1. What is Conditional Rendering?

React ‡¶è **Conditional Rendering** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ (conditions) ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé, ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component UI ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, user login ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ profile ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá login form ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. Importance of Conditional Rendering

React ‡¶è **Conditional Rendering** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Web application ‡¶è user ‡¶è‡¶∞ interaction, data ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á dynamic ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø Conditional Rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø e-commerce site ‡¶è user logged in ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ order history ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ logged in ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá login ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ì, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã API call ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® loader ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ result ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. Different Ways to Implement Conditional Rendering

#### Using if/else Statements

Traditional **if/else** statement ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá React ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á conditional rendering ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á statements JSX ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  if (props.isLoggedIn) {
    return <h1>Welcome back!</h1>;
  } else {
    return <h1>Please sign up.</h1>;
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(
  <Greeting isLoggedIn={true} />,
  document.getElementById("root")
);
```

#### Breakdown:

- **if/else Statement**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **props.isLoggedIn** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Welcome back!" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Please sign up."‡•§
- Output:
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **"Welcome back!"**
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** false ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **"Please sign up."**

#### Using Ternary Operators

**Ternary operator** React ‡¶è conditional rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  return (
    <div>
      {props.isLoggedIn ? <h1>Welcome back!</h1> : <h1>Please sign up.</h1>}
    </div>
  );
}

ReactDOM.render(
  <Greeting isLoggedIn={false} />,
  document.getElementById("root")
);
```

#### Breakdown:

- **Ternary Operator**: ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá condition check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá "Welcome back!" ‡¶¨‡¶æ "Please sign up." ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Output:
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **"Welcome back!"**
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** false ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **"Please sign up."**

#### Using Logical && Operator

**Logical && operator** React ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  return <div>{props.isLoggedIn && <h1>Welcome back!</h1>}</div>;
}

ReactDOM.render(
  <Greeting isLoggedIn={true} />,
  document.getElementById("root")
);
```

#### Breakdown:

- **Logical && operator**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **props.isLoggedIn** true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Welcome back!" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø false ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶á render ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Output:
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **"Welcome back!"**
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn** false ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º: **(‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ)**

#### Using Switch Statements

‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **switch statement** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º conditions ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function Greeting(props) {
  switch (props.status) {
    case "guest":
      return <h1>Welcome, Guest!</h1>;
    case "user":
      return <h1>Welcome back!</h1>;
    case "admin":
      return <h1>Welcome, Admin!</h1>;
    default:
      return <h1>Hello!</h1>;
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(<Greeting status="admin" />, document.getElementById("root"));
```

#### Breakdown:

- **Switch Statement**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **props.status** ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® greeting message ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, guest ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø "Welcome, Guest!" ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç admin ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø "Welcome, Admin!"‡•§
- Output:
  - **status** "admin" ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá: **"Welcome, Admin!"**
  - **status** "guest" ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá: **"Welcome, Guest!"**
  - ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã status ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá: **"Hello!"**

---

### 4. Real-life Example of Conditional Rendering

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **E-commerce Dashboard** ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user logged in ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç recent order ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ logged in ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá login ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

##### Example:

```jsx
function UserDashboard(props) {
  if (props.isLoggedIn) {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Welcome back, {props.userName}!</h1>
        <p>Here are your recent orders:</p>
        {/* Order details */}
      </div>
    );
  } else {
    return (
      <div>
        <h1>Please log in to view your dashboard.</h1>
        <button onClick={props.onLogin}>Login</button>
      </div>
    );
  }
}

ReactDOM.render(
  <UserDashboard
    isLoggedIn={false}
    userName="John"
    onLogin={() => alert("Logging in...")}
  />,
  document.getElementById("root")
);
```

#### Breakdown:

- **isLoggedIn ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá**: ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø user logged in ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç order details ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá login button ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **Output**:
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn = true** ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá:
    ```
    Welcome back, John!
    Here are your recent orders.
    ```
  - ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø **isLoggedIn = false** ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá:
    ```
    Please log in to view your dashboard.
    [Login Button]
    ```

---

### 5. Best Practices for Conditional Rendering

1. **Simple Logic ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**: Complex conditional rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **ternary operator** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **&& operator** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü condition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï **if/else** ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **ternary operator** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§
2. **Nested JSX ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶®**: Nested JSX ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã subcomponents ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

3. **Switch Statement ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® **switch statement** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. Conclusion

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Conditional Rendering** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI ‡¶ï‡ßá dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç responsive ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø user ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¨‡¶æ props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§ React ‡¶è conditional rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **if/else**, **ternary operators**, **&& operator**, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **switch statement**‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø situation ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

# Chapter-11.1: React List & Keys

## Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to Lists & Keys](#introduction-to-lists--keys)
2. [Why Use Lists & Keys in React?](#why-use-lists--keys-in-react)

5. [Examples - Beginner to Advanced](#examples---beginner-to-advanced)
6. [Best Practices for Lists & Keys](#best-practices-for-lists--keys)

---

### 1. üìò Introduction to Lists & Keys

React ‡¶è **Lists** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **Keys** concepts component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Lists React ‡¶ï‡ßá multiple similar data items manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Keys React ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶ï‡ßá track ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

---

### 2. üßê Why Use Lists & Keys in React?

React ‡¶è lists ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç keys ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient data rendering ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- **Dynamic Data Handling**: Lists ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá dynamic content ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Optimized Rendering**: Keys ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá React component update ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç re-render efficiently manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. üîÑ Rendering Lists with the `map()` Function

React ‡¶è list rendering ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `map()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® array return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element ‡¶ï‡ßá React element ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
const items = ["Apple", "Banana", "Cherry"];

function ItemList() {
  return (
    <ul>
      {items.map((item) => (
        <li>{item}</li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}
```

---

### 4. üóùÔ∏è Understanding Keys in React

Keys React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø unique identifiers ‡¶Ø‡¶æ list items ‡¶è‡¶∞ re-rendering efficiency ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Keys unique ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç stable ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® React ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá items track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 5. üìñ Examples - Beginner to Advanced

---

#### Example 1: Basic List Rendering with Keys (Beginner)

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple list render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø unique key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React from "react";

const fruits = [
  { id: 1, name: "Apple" },
  { id: 2, name: "Banana" },
  { id: 3, name: "Cherry" },
];

function FruitList() {
  return (
    <ul>
      {fruits.map((fruit) => (
        <li key={fruit.id}>{fruit.name}</li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}

export default FruitList;
```

**Explanation**:

- `fruits` array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶ï‡ßá `id` attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá key ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá React efficiently items track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unnecessary re-renders ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 2: Dynamic List with Conditional Rendering (Intermediate)

Dynamic data ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç conditional rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡•§

```javascript
import React from "react";

const products = [
  { id: 101, name: "Laptop", price: 999.99, isAvailable: true },
  { id: 102, name: "Smartphone", price: 699.99, isAvailable: false },
  { id: 103, name: "Tablet", price: 499.99, isAvailable: true },
];

function ProductList() {
  return (
    <ul>
      {products.map((product) => (
        <li key={product.id}>
          <h3>{product.name}</h3>
          <p>Price: ${product.price}</p>
          <p>
            {product.isAvailable ? (
              <span style={{ color: "green" }}>In Stock</span>
            ) : (
              <span style={{ color: "red" }}>Out of Stock</span>
            )}
          </p>
        </li>
      ))}
    </ul>
  );
}

export default ProductList;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Nested Data**: `products` array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶è name, price, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç availability status ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Conditional Rendering**: Availability ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá stock status green ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ red color ‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Unique Key**: `id` ‡¶ï‡ßá key ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ React ‡¶ï‡ßá items efficiently track ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 3: List Rendering from API Data (Advanced)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø external API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ list ‡¶è render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

```javascript
import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";

function UserList() {
  const [users, setUsers] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch("https://jsonplaceholder.typicode.com/users")
      .then((response) => response.json())
      .then((data) => setUsers(data))
      .catch((error) => console.error("Error fetching data:", error));
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h2>User List</h2>
      <ul>
        {users.map((user) => (
          <li key={user.id}>
            <h3>{user.name}</h3>
            <p>Email: {user.email}</p>
          </li>
        ))}
      </ul>
    </div>
  );
}

export default UserList;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Data Fetching**: API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `users` state ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Unique Keys with API Data**: API ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ data ‡¶è‡¶∞ `id` ‡¶ï‡ßá unique key ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Real-Time Update**: Data fetch ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ `users` state update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI ‡¶§‡ßá list render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 6. ‚úÖ Best Practices for Lists & Keys

1. **Use Unique and Stable Keys**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø unique `id` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
2. **Avoid Using Array Index**: Index ‡¶ï‡ßá key ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø list ‡¶è‡¶∞ order ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Use `map()` for Lists**: `map()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá lists render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ React ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø common practice‡•§
4. **Avoid Inline Key Generation Functions**: Inline functions performance ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á avoid ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

---

### ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶™‡ßá

React ‡¶è Lists ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Keys application ‡¶è‡¶∞ efficiency ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manageability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Keys ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá React effectively items track ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unnecessary re-renders ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Properly managed lists ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç keys ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá React application ‡¶è‡¶∞ performance ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainability ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
