    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-11.2: üìã React Form Handling - Controlled vs Uncontrolled Components

## Table of Contents

1. [Introduction to Form Handling in React](#introduction-to-form-handling-in-react)
2. [What are Controlled Components?](#what-are-controlled-components)
3. [What are Uncontrolled Components?](#what-are-uncontrolled-components)
4. [Controlled vs Uncontrolled Components - Key Differences](#controlled-vs-uncontrolled-components---key-differences)
5. [Examples of Controlled and Uncontrolled Components](#examples-of-controlled-and-uncontrolled-components)
6. [Best Practices in Form Handling](#best-practices-in-form-handling)

---

### 1. üìò Introduction to Form Handling in React

React ‡¶è form handling user input ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡•§ React ‡¶è form handling ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:

- **Controlled Components**: ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ data React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Uncontrolled Components**: ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ data ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡•§ Controlled ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Uncontrolled Components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ React ‡¶è form handling ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. üìù What are Controlled Components?

**Controlled Components** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React component ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ values ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡ßá synchronized ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

#### Key Points:

- Form values React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `onChange` event trigger ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶æ state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá React UI ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡ßá synchronized ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§

#### Example: Controlled Component

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function ControlledForm() {
  const [name, setName] = useState("");

  const handleChange = (event) => {
    setName(event.target.value);
  };

  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    console.log("Submitted name:", name);
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <label>
        Name:
        <input type="text" value={name} onChange={handleChange} />
      </label>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default ControlledForm;
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ**:

- `name` state variable form input ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `handleChange` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ input field ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡¶≤‡ßá `name` state update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `value={name}` attribute input ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Controlled Component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 3. üîç What are Uncontrolled Components?

**Uncontrolled Components** ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá form ‡¶è‡¶∞ values ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º `ref` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá data React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø traditional HTML form ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Key Points:

- Form values React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Input fields ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `ref` attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá values access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ forms ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ third-party libraries ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá Uncontrolled Components ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§

#### Example: Uncontrolled Component

```javascript
import React, { useRef } from "react";

function UncontrolledForm() {
  const nameRef = useRef();

  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    console.log("Submitted name:", nameRef.current.value);
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <label>
        Name:
        <input type="text" ref={nameRef} />
      </label>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default UncontrolledForm;
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ**:

- `nameRef` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `ref` attribute ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá input field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã `onChange` handler ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç `nameRef.current.value` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá input field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### 4. üîÑ Controlled vs Uncontrolled Components - Key Differences

| ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø                | Controlled Components                       | Uncontrolled Components                                             |
| ------------------------ | ------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Data Handling**        | React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§           | ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º                                      |
| **Control Over Input**   | React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá      | DOM ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§                                          |
| **Real-time Validation** | ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ data ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø state ‡¶è ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá | ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ values `ref` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º                   |
| **Use Case**             | Dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç complex forms                   | Simple forms ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ third-party libraries ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§             |
| **Performance**          | ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ß‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ state ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞    | ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º |

---

### 5. üìñ Examples of Controlled and Uncontrolled Components

---

#### Example 1: Controlled Component with Multiple Inputs

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø form ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá multiple input fields ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá (name ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç email), ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® React ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function ControlledMultiInputForm() {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    name: "",
    email: "",
  });

  const handleChange = (event) => {
    const { name, value } = event.target;
    setFormData((prevData) => ({
      ...prevData,
      [name]: value,
    }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    console.log("Form Data:", formData);
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <label>
        Name:
        <input
          type="text"
          name="name"
          value={formData.name}
          onChange={handleChange}
        />
      </label>
      <label>
        Email:
        <input
          type="email"
          name="email"
          value={formData.email}
          onChange={handleChange}
        />
      </label>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default ControlledMultiInputForm;
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ**:

- `formData` state ‡¶è `name` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `email` values ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `handleChange` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® dynamically state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø input ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá synchronized ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 2: Uncontrolled Component with Multiple Inputs

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá multiple input fields ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá `ref` attribute ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React, { useRef } from "react";

function UncontrolledMultiInputForm() {
  const nameRef = useRef();
  const emailRef = useRef();

  const handleSubmit = (event) => {
    event.preventDefault();
    console.log("Submitted Name:", nameRef.current.value);
    console.log("Submitted Email:", emailRef.current.value);
  };

  return (
    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
      <label>
        Name:
        <input type="text" ref={nameRef} />
      </label>
      <label>
        Email:
        <input type="email" ref={emailRef} />
      </label>
      <button type="submit">Submit</button>
    </form>
  );
}

export default UncontrolledMultiInputForm;
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ**:

- `nameRef` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `emailRef` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø input values access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Uncontrolled Components ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§

---

### 6. ‚úÖ Best Practices in Form Handling

1. **Complex Forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Controlled Components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**: Dynamic forms ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá validation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç real-time updates ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá controlled components ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§
2. **Simple Forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Uncontrolled Components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®**: ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá uncontrolled components ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§
3. **Separate Components for Better Management**: ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ component ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá consider ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡•§
4. **Avoid Mixing Controlled and Uncontrolled Approaches**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡ßá controlled ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç uncontrolled ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ behavior ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### Summary

React ‡¶è **Controlled Components** state ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá form data manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá **Uncontrolled Components** ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø DOM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Complex ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamic forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø controlled components ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá simple forms ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá uncontrolled components ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç efficient‡•§ Controlled ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Uncontrolled ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ form handling ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ üòä

---

### 1. üìò Introduction to Lifting State Up

**Lifting State Up** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá state ‡¶ï‡ßá component tree ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø higher level ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï child component ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á state access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è reflect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® state ‡¶ï‡ßá parent ‡¶¨‡¶æ common ancestor component ‡¶è move ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá lifting state up ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### State Lifting ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ:

- **Centralized State Management**: State ‡¶ï‡ßá common ancestor component ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ child component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data consistency ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç synchronization ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Component Communication**: Lifting state up parent-child component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data passing ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### 2. üßê Why Use Lifting State Up?

React ‡¶è lifting state up ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **data synchronization** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **consistent UI**‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Consistent Data Across Components**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á data ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® lifting state up ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá synchronized data ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Improves Data Flow**: Component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data flow ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Centralized State Management**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ state ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá state ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
4. **Easier Data Sharing**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è data flow ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç synchronization ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 3. üîç How Lifting State Up Works in React

#### Steps for Lifting State Up:

1. **Identify Shared State**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® state ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Move State to Parent Component**: Shared state ‡¶ï‡ßá parent component ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø common ancestor ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. **Pass State and Update Function as Props**: Parent component ‡¶è‡¶∞ state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update function ‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
4. **Use Props in Child Components**: Child component ‡¶è parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

### 4. üìñ Examples - Beginner to Advanced

---

#### Example 1: Synchronized Temperature Inputs (Beginner)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø temperature converter ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Celsius ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Fahrenheit ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá conversion ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ü‡¶ø automatically update ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ lifting state up ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá temperature data ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç conversion logic centralize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

##### Step 1: TemperatureInput Component

```javascript
import React from "react";

function TemperatureInput({ scale, temperature, onTemperatureChange }) {
  const scaleNames = { c: "Celsius", f: "Fahrenheit" };

  const handleChange = (event) => {
    onTemperatureChange(event.target.value);
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <label>Enter temperature in {scaleNames[scale]}:</label>
      <input value={temperature} onChange={handleChange} />
    </div>
  );
}

export default TemperatureInput;
```

**Explanation**:

- `TemperatureInput` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reusable component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `scale` (Celsius ‡¶¨‡¶æ Fahrenheit), `temperature` (temperature value), ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `onTemperatureChange` (temperature update function) props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `handleChange` function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá temperature ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `onTemperatureChange` function call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Step 2: Temperature Conversion Functions

```javascript
function toCelsius(fahrenheit) {
  return ((fahrenheit - 32) * 5) / 9;
}

function toFahrenheit(celsius) {
  return (celsius * 9) / 5 + 32;
}

export { toCelsius, toFahrenheit };
```

**Explanation**:

- `toCelsius` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `toFahrenheit` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Fahrenheit ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Celsius ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Celsius ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Fahrenheit ‡¶è temperature conversion ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Step 3: TemperatureCalculator Parent Component

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";
import TemperatureInput from "./TemperatureInput";
import { toCelsius, toFahrenheit } from "./conversions";

function TemperatureCalculator() {
  const [temperature, setTemperature] = useState("");
  const [scale, setScale] = useState("c");

  const handleCelsiusChange = (temp) => {
    setTemperature(temp);
    setScale("c");
  };

  const handleFahrenheitChange = (temp) => {
    setTemperature(temp);
    setScale("f");
  };

  const celsius = scale === "f" ? toCelsius(temperature) : temperature;
  const fahrenheit = scale === "c" ? toFahrenheit(temperature) : temperature;

  return (
    <div>
      <TemperatureInput
        scale="c"
        temperature={celsius}
        onTemperatureChange={handleCelsiusChange}
      />
      <TemperatureInput
        scale="f"
        temperature={fahrenheit}
        onTemperatureChange={handleFahrenheitChange}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

export default TemperatureCalculator;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Lifting State Up**: `temperature` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `scale` state ‡¶ï‡ßá common parent component `TemperatureCalculator` ‡¶è initialize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Passing Props**: `TemperatureInput` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá `temperature`, `scale`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `onTemperatureChange` props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Data Synchronization**: `TemperatureInput` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá input temperature change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `handleCelsiusChange` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `handleFahrenheitChange` function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ updated temperature value ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scale set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ State change ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá parent component `TemperatureCalculator` re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø input field ‡¶è updated value display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 2: Shopping Cart Quantity Sync (Intermediate)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø shopping cart ‡¶è item quantity update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø input field ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç total quantity display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ State lift ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ quantity update ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç display ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá sync ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

##### Step 1: QuantityInput Component

```javascript
import React from "react";

function QuantityInput({ quantity, onQuantityChange }) {
  return (
    <input
      type="number"
      value={quantity}
      onChange={(e) => onQuantityChange(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}
    />
  );
}

export default QuantityInput;
```

**Explanation**:

- `QuantityInput` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø input component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ quantity input ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `onQuantityChange` function call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá parent component ‡¶è quantity ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Step 2: CartDisplay Component

```javascript
import React from "react";

function CartDisplay({ quantity }) {
  return <p>Total Quantity: {quantity}</p>;
}

export default CartDisplay;
```

**Explanation**:

- `CartDisplay` component ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ total quantity display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Quantity value props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá parent component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

##### Step 3: ShoppingCart Parent Component

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";
import QuantityInput from "./QuantityInput";
import CartDisplay from "./CartDisplay";

function ShoppingCart() {
  const [quantity, setQuantity] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div>
      <QuantityInput quantity={quantity} onQuantityChange={setQuantity} />
      <CartDisplay quantity={quantity} />
    </div>
  );
}

export default ShoppingCart;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Lifting State Up**: `quantity` state ‡¶ï‡ßá `ShoppingCart` component ‡¶è lift ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Passing Props**: `QuantityInput` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `CartDisplay` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá `quantity` state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setQuantity` function pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **State Synchronization**: User quantity update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `setQuantity` call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ updated quantity `CartDisplay` component ‡¶è automatically reflect ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 3: Form Input Sync with Validation (Advanced)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø multi-field form ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® input field ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data synchronization ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç validation ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡•§

##### Step 1: FormInput Component

```javascript
import React from "react";

function FormInput({ label, value, onChange, error }) {
  return (
    <div>
      <label>{label}</label>
      <input value={value} onChange={onChange} />
      {error && <p style={{ color: "red" }}>{error}</p>}
    </div>
  );
}

export default FormInput;
```

**Explanation**:

- `FormInput` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø reusable component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `label`, `value`, `onChange`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `error` props ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Error ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø error message display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

##### Step 2: Parent Form Component with Validation

```javascript
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import FormInput from './Form

Input';

function Form() {
  const [username, setUsername] = useState("");
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState({ username: "", email: "" });

  const handleUsernameChange = (e) => {
    const value = e.target.value;
    setUsername(value);
    setErrors((prevErrors) => ({
      ...prevErrors,
      username: value.length < 3 ? "Username must be at least 3 characters." : ""
    }));
  };

  const handleEmailChange = (e) => {
    const value = e.target.value;
    setEmail(value);
    setErrors((prevErrors) => ({
      ...prevErrors,
      email: value.includes("@") ? "" : "Email must include @."
    }));
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <FormInput
        label="Username"
        value={username}
        onChange={handleUsernameChange}
        error={errors.username}
      />
      <FormInput
        label="Email"
        value={email}
        onChange={handleEmailChange}
        error={errors.email}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

export default Form;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Lifting State Up**: `username`, `email`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `errors` state ‡¶ï‡ßá parent component `Form` ‡¶è lift ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Passing Props for Synchronization and Validation**: `FormInput` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá value, onChange function, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç error message props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Real-Time Validation**: User input change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá validation check ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç error message update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Updated value ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç error message `FormInput` ‡¶è synchronize ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### 5. ‚úÖ Best Practices for Lifting State Up

1. **Identify Shared Data**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® data ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§
2. **Avoid Unnecessary Lifting**: ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º data lift ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ state lift ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá code structure unnecessarily complex ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Pass Only Required Props**: Child component ‡¶è ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º props pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶≤ data flow ‡¶¨‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
4. **Keep Components Modular**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá state management ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá child component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá modular ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

### Summary

React ‡¶è **Lifting State Up** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ pattern ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data sync ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç consistent UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§ Properly managed lifted state ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React application ‡¶è‡¶∞ data flow ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data sharing structure ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

# Chapter-12: üìã React Inheritance

---

### üìò Introduction to React Inheritance

React ‡¶è **Inheritance** concept ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá discouraged ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Inheritance ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé parent-child class relationship traditional Object-Oriented Programming (OOP) ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá parent class ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶¨‡¶æ methods child class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ design philosophy ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ component composition (composition over inheritance) ‡¶ï‡ßá encourage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã nested ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø props ‡¶ì context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ composition ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá component ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ, code structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular, flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

---

### üßê Why React Prefers Composition Over Inheritance

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá composition ‡¶ï‡ßá inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Code Reusability**: Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® layout ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component nesting ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§
2. **Loose Coupling**: Composition ‡¶è component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã parent-child relationship ‡¶è‡¶∞ strict binding ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ more flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Easy Debugging**: Composition structure ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá debugging ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintenance ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Flexible Structure**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç customization ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### üîç Understanding the Limitations of Inheritance in React

React ‡¶è inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ limitation ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø discouraged:

1. **Complex Structure**: Inheritance ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã tightly-coupled ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component tree structure complex ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Less Flexibility**: Inheritance ‡¶è component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã parent class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ independent ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **Prop Management Complexity**: Inheritance ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá prop management ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data flow control ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
4. **Limited Use Cases**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá inheritance ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶∂‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç context data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable‡•§

---

### üõ†Ô∏è Alternatives to Inheritance in React

React ‡¶è inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá code structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶™ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

#### 1. **Component Composition**

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá component composition ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§ Component composition ‡¶è, ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component nested ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Composition ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ UI structure ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á modular ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example of Composition**:

```javascript
function Header() {
  return <header>Header</header>;
}

function Footer() {
  return <footer>Footer</footer>;
}

function Layout({ children }) {
  return (
    <div>
      <Header />
      {children}
      <Footer />
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Layout>
      <main>Main Content</main>
    </Layout>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `Header` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Footer` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã `Layout` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá composition ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `Layout` component ‡¶è `children` prop ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá main content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá reusable UI structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### 2. **Higher-Order Components (HOCs)**

**Higher-Order Components (HOCs)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® behavior ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá reusable logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

**Example of HOC**:

```javascript
import React from "react";

function withLogger(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent(props) {
    console.log("Rendering:", WrappedComponent.name);
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}

function MyComponent() {
  return <div>Hello, World!</div>;
}

const EnhancedComponent = withLogger(MyComponent);
```

**Explanation**:

- `withLogger` HOC `MyComponent` ‡¶ï‡ßá enhanced ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- HOCs ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá inheritance ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á reusable behavior ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

#### 3. **Render Props**

Render props ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá parent component ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ data ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç behavior child component ‡¶è props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§

**Example of Render Props**:

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Counter({ render }) {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
  return render(count, () => setCount(count + 1));
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Counter
      render={(count, increment) => (
        <div>
          <p>Count: {count}</p>
          <button onClick={increment}>Increment</button>
        </div>
      )}
    />
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `Counter` component ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ behavior `render` props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá child component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Render props inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá data ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§

---

### üìñ Real-life Examples of Composition vs. Inheritance

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Example 1: Authentication Layout (Using Composition)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø application ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá login ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logout layout ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§

```javascript
function Header() {
  return <header>Header</header>;
}

function Footer() {
  return <footer>Footer</footer>;
}

function AuthLayout({ children }) {
  return (
    <div>
      <Header />
      {children}
      <Footer />
    </div>
  );
}

function Login() {
  return (
    <AuthLayout>
      <div>Login Form</div>
    </AuthLayout>
  );
}

function Logout() {
  return (
    <AuthLayout>
      <div>Logout Confirmation</div>
    </AuthLayout>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `AuthLayout` component composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá common `Header` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Footer` ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `Login` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Logout` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã `AuthLayout` ‡¶ï‡ßá reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Example 2: Applying Permissions (Using HOC Instead of Inheritance)

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø application ‡¶è permission check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
function withPermissionCheck(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent(props) {
    const hasPermission = /* permission logic */;
    if (!hasPermission) return <div>Access Denied</div>;
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}

function Dashboard() {
  return <div>Dashboard Content</div>;
}

const ProtectedDashboard = withPermissionCheck(Dashboard);
```

**Explanation**:

- `withPermissionCheck` HOC `Dashboard` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø permission check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Dashboard` ‡¶ï‡ßá enhanced ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- HOC inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá behavior enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices

React ‡¶è inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø pattern ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Best Practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

1. **Use Composition Over Inheritance**: React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá component nesting ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§
2. **Implement HOCs for Reusable Behavior**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á behavior ‡¶¨‡¶æ feature ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. **Use Render Props for Shared Logic**: Component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá render props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ flexibility ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Avoid Tight Coupling**: Component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá loosely coupled ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code structure ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

React ‡¶è inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç context, HOCs, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç render props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá code structure ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Proper usage ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá React application ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá‡•§

---

### üìò Introduction to Composition in React

**Composition** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful pattern ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá nested structure ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá parent-child relationship ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá code ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç behavior reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç UI structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã modular, maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá complex UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ design philosophy ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ, composition ‡¶ï‡ßá inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Composition parent component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø child component ‡¶ï‡ßá customize ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç re-use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

---

### üßê Why Use Composition in React?

React ‡¶è composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **Code Reusability**: Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
2. **Flexible and Modular Structure**: Component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá nested structure ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ UI structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **Loose Coupling**: Composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã loosely coupled ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã tightly coupled ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
4. **Enhanced Readability**: Composition ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ structure ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶°‡¶º‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ debugging ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintenance ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üîç Implementing Composition in React

Composition implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø React ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá `children` props, named props, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç specialized components ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® implementation approach ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### üìÇ Common Patterns of Composition

#### 1. Children Props

React ‡¶è **`children` props** ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ composition ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá parent component ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ child component ‡¶ï‡ßá `children` props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá parent component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example of Children Props**:

```javascript
function Card({ children }) {
  return <div className="card">{children}</div>;
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Card>
      <h2>Card Title</h2>
      <p>This is a card description.</p>
    </Card>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `Card` component `children` props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá nested content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `App` component ‡¶è `Card` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá `h2` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `p` elements `children` props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `children` props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component structure ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### 2. Props for Dynamic Content

‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã `children` props ‡¶Ø‡¶•‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü content dynamically inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá specific content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ composition ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì dynamic ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç customizable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

**Example of Dynamic Props**:

```javascript
function Dialog({ title, content }) {
  return (
    <div className="dialog">
      <h2>{title}</h2>
      <p>{content}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <Dialog title="Welcome" content="This is a welcome message." />
      <Dialog title="Goodbye" content="Thank you for visiting!" />
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `Dialog` component `title` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `content` props ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® context ‡¶è re-use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `App` component ‡¶è `Dialog` component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component structure ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### 3. Specialized Components

Composition ‡¶è **Specialized Components** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá context-specific ‡¶¨‡¶æ layout-specific components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá parent component ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá section ‡¶¨‡¶æ slot ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç structure ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Example of Specialized Components**:

```javascript
function Layout({ header, sidebar, content }) {
  return (
    <div className="layout">
      <header>{header}</header>
      <aside>{sidebar}</aside>
      <main>{content}</main>
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Layout
      header={<h1>Website Header</h1>}
      sidebar={<p>Sidebar Content</p>}
      content={<p>Main Content Area</p>}
    />
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `Layout` component ‡¶è `header`, `sidebar`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `content` props ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ layout ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§
- `App` component ‡¶è `Layout` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü content pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ composition ‡¶ï‡ßá structured ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üìñ Real-life Examples of Composition

#### Example 1: Modal Component with Composition

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø modal component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® context ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
function Modal({ title, children }) {
  return (
    <div className="modal">
      <h2>{title}</h2>
      <div className="modal-content">{children}</div>
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <Modal title="Confirmation">
        <p>Are you sure you want to proceed?</p>
        <button>Yes</button>
        <button>No</button>
      </Modal>
      <Modal title="Notification">
        <p>You have a new message.</p>
      </Modal>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Modal Component**: `Modal` component `title` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `children` props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá content display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **App Component**: `App` component ‡¶è `Modal` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® context ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Output**: Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `Modal` component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® layout ‡¶è content display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá flexible ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

#### Example 2: Navbar Layout with Composition

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø application ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá Navbar ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® section ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§

```javascript
function Navbar({ logo, menu, profile }) {
  return (
    <nav className="navbar">
      <div className="navbar-logo">{logo}</div>
      <div className="navbar-menu">{menu}</div>
      <div className="navbar-profile">{profile}</div>
    </nav>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <Navbar
      logo={<img src="logo.png" alt="Logo" />}
      menu={
        <ul>
          <li>Home</li>
          <li>About</li>
          <li>Contact</li>
        </ul>
      }
      profile={<button>Login</button>}
    />
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Navbar Component**: `Navbar` component `logo`, `menu`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `profile` props ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **App Component**: `App` component ‡¶è `Navbar` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® section ‡¶è content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Output**: Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `Navbar` component ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices for Composition in React

Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Best Practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§:

1. **Use Composition Over Inheritance**: React ‡¶è inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component structure ‡¶ï‡ßá simple ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Avoid Nested Composition if Possible**: ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ nested composition structure ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á nesting ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
3. **Use Meaningful Names for Props**: Composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø meaningful ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç descriptive props ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Use `children` for Flexible Structure**: `children` props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá nested structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ content inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

React ‡¶è Composition ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ structure ‡¶ï‡ßá modular ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Proper usage ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá React application ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá‡•§

</div>

# Chapter-12.2: üìã React Inheritance vs Composition - Detailed Example with Tight Coupling Explanation

### Introduction

React ‡¶è Composition ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® composition ‡¶è **Tight Coupling** ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶ö inheritance structure ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá tight coupling ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### Tight Coupling vs Loose Coupling

- **Tight Coupling**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶¨‡¶æ class ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶¨‡¶æ class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶á component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã tightly coupled‡•§
- **Loose Coupling**: Loose coupling ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï component ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ React ‡¶è composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á loose coupling ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## Example: Inheritance vs Composition

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `Notification` component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ notification display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

1. Success Notification
2. Error Notification
3. Warning Notification

‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á component ‡¶¶‡ßÅ'‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá inheritance ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ flexibility ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ tight coupling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

---

### Using Inheritance (Tight Coupling Example)

Inheritance structure ‡¶è, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø `Notification` base class ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ notification ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø subclass ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

```javascript
import React from "react";

// Base Notification Class
class Notification extends React.Component {
  renderIcon() {
    return <span>üîî</span>; // Default icon
  }

  renderMessage() {
    return <p>Notification message</p>;
  }

  render() {
    return (
      <div className="notification">
        {this.renderIcon()}
        {this.renderMessage()}
      </div>
    );
  }
}

// Success Notification (Subclass)
class SuccessNotification extends Notification {
  renderIcon() {
    return <span>‚úÖ</span>; // Success icon
  }

  renderMessage() {
    return <p>Success! Your operation completed successfully.</p>;
  }
}

// Error Notification (Subclass)
class ErrorNotification extends Notification {
  renderIcon() {
    return <span>‚ùå</span>; // Error icon
  }

  renderMessage() {
    return <p>Error! Something went wrong.</p>;
  }
}

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <SuccessNotification />
      <ErrorNotification />
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Base Class**: `Notification` base class ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá default icon ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç message ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Subclasses**: `SuccessNotification` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `ErrorNotification` ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø subclass, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `Notification` class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á subclass ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá `renderIcon` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `renderMessage` method override ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Tight Coupling**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá subclasses ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã base class `Notification` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `Notification` class ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® element ‡¶¨‡¶æ styling ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º), ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `SuccessNotification` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `ErrorNotification` ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ subclass ‡¶è‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Limitations of Inheritance (Tight Coupling)

- **Fixed Structure**: `Notification` ‡¶è‡¶∞ subclasses ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ structure base class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ notification ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® subclass ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **Limited Flexibility**: Subclass ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã tightly coupled ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá easily customize ‡¶¨‡¶æ change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶®‡•§
- **Dependency on Base Class**: `Notification` class ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ subclass ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ tight coupling ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ subclass ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø base class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡•§

---

### Using Composition (Loose Coupling Example)

Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ `Notification` component ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç loosely coupled ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá `Notification` component ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ layout/container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content dynamically inject ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React from "react";

// Base Notification Component using Composition
function Notification({ icon, message }) {
  return (
    <div className="notification">
      <span>{icon}</span>
      <p>{message}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

// Success Notification Component
function SuccessNotification() {
  return (
    <Notification
      icon="‚úÖ"
      message="Success! Your operation completed successfully."
    />
  );
}

// Error Notification Component
function ErrorNotification() {
  return <Notification icon="‚ùå" message="Error! Something went wrong." />;
}

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <SuccessNotification />
      <ErrorNotification />
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Base Component**: `Notification` component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø generic layout ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `icon` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `message` props ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá component ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® content ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Dynamic Content**: `SuccessNotification` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `ErrorNotification` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ content pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `Notification` component ‡¶ï‡ßá customize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Loose Coupling**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `Notification` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ `SuccessNotification` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `ErrorNotification` component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá content pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá customize ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `Notification` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì child component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã unaffected ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### Why Composition is Better than Inheritance in React

1. **Loose Coupling**:

   - **Composition**: Composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá loose coupling ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ `Notification` component ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç `icon` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `message` props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá dynamically content pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - **Inheritance**: Inheritance structure ‡¶è subclass ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã tightly coupled ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ base class ‡¶è‡¶∞ properties ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç methods directly inherit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Base class ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá subclass ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

2. **Flexibility and Reusability**:

   - **Composition**: Composition ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `Notification` component reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ notification (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Warning ‡¶¨‡¶æ Info) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ inheritance structure ‡¶è subclass ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - **Inheritance**: Inheritance structure ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ notification ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ subclass ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá code duplication ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexibility ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

3. **Maintainable and Clear Structure**:

   - **Composition**: Composition structure inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Composition structure predictable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç changes implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡•§
   - **Inheritance**: Inheritance ‡¶è subclass structure ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç base class ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ subclass ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø code structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç less maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

4. **Avoids Code Duplication**:
   - **Composition**: Composition structure ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á `Notification` component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® content ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá re-use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code duplication ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - **Inheritance**: Inheritance structure ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ layout ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® subclass ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ code duplication ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### Summary

React ‡¶è Composition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component structure ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç loosely coupled ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Composition inheritance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable structure ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ Properly implemented composition structure component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá modular, clean ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç React ‡¶è‡¶∞ declarative nature ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

# Chapter-13: React Higher Order Components (HOC)

### Table of Contents

1. [üåü What is a Higher Order Component (HOC)?](#what-is-a-higher-order-component-hoc)
2. [üßê Why Use Higher Order Components?](#why-use-higher-order-components)
3. [‚öôÔ∏è How HOCs Work](#how-hocs-work)
4. [üöÄ Implementing HOCs in React](#implementing-hocs-in-react)
5. [üîç Examples of Higher Order Components](#examples-of-higher-order-components)
6. [‚úÖ Best Practices for HOCs](#best-practices-for-hocs)

---

### 1. üåü What is a Higher Order Component (HOC)?

A **Higher Order Component (HOC)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø advanced technique ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **JavaScript function** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **React component** ‡¶ï‡ßá argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ HOC component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dynamically configurable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø basic component ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ data render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á component ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø loading indicator ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ loading feature ‡¶ü‡¶ø main component ‡¶è ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

- Component ‡¶ï‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
- ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® functionality ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
- Component ‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡¶æ

**Example Structure**:

```javascript
const EnhancedComponent = higherOrderComponent(OriginalComponent);
```

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá, `higherOrderComponent` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `OriginalComponent` ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® `EnhancedComponent` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 2. üßê Why Use Higher Order Components?

React ‡¶è HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶É‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modularity ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### a. **Code Reuse**

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á functionality ‡¶¨‡¶æ logic ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á logic ‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡¶¨ component ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø loading feature ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á loading feature ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è add ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

#### b. **Separation of Concerns**

HOCs component ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá **Separation of Concerns** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ logic ‡¶ï‡¶Æplex ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç readability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, authentication check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç authentication logic ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

#### c. **Conditional Rendering**

‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶¨‡¶æ props ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá HOC ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§ HOCs component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ feature conditionally ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡•§

#### d. **Enhancement without Modification**

HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶¨‡¶æ functionality ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® feature ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø React ‡¶è‡¶∞ **Pure Functions** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

### 3. ‚öôÔ∏è How HOCs Work

Higher Order Component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá argument ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø props ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶ï‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Example Code Structure

```javascript
function withExtraFunctionality(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent(props) {
    // ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ extra ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `withExtraFunctionality` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï function ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá `WrappedComponent` component ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `EnhancedComponent` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶ï‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `{...props}` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ props retain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá enhanced component ‡¶∏‡¶¨ props access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### 4. üöÄ Implementing HOCs in React

React ‡¶è HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ code reusability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

#### Implementing a Loading Indicator HOC

```javascript
import React from "react";

function withLoadingIndicator(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent({ isLoading, ...props }) {
    if (isLoading) return <p>Loading...</p>;
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}
```

**Explanation**:

1. **HOC Definition**: `withLoadingIndicator` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `WrappedComponent` ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Conditional Rendering**: `isLoading` prop check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ `isLoading` true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá "Loading..." ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Main Component Render**: `isLoading` false ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ `WrappedComponent` render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á `withLoadingIndicator` HOC ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ loading feature ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

### 5. üîç Examples of Higher Order Components

#### Example 1: Loading Indicator with HOC

```javascript
import React from "react";

function withLoadingIndicator(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent({ isLoading, ...props }) {
    if (isLoading) return <p>Loading...</p>;
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}

function DataDisplay({ data }) {
  return <div>Data: {data}</div>;
}

const DataDisplayWithLoading = withLoadingIndicator(DataDisplay);

// Usage in App
function App() {
  return <DataDisplayWithLoading isLoading={true} data="Some Data" />;
}
```

**Detailed Explanation**:

1. **withLoadingIndicator HOC**: ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `isLoading` prop ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `isLoading` true ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø "Loading..." ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **DataDisplay Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ component, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `data` props ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple message render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Enhanced Component**: `DataDisplayWithLoading` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `DataDisplay` ‡¶ï‡ßá `withLoadingIndicator` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá enhanced ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Usage**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® `isLoading={true}` ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® "Loading..." ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ `isLoading` false ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá `DataDisplay` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ content ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example 2: Authorization HOC

```javascript
import React from "react";

function withAuthorization(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent({ isAuthenticated, ...props }) {
    if (!isAuthenticated)
      return <p>You are not authorized to view this content.</p>;
    return <WrappedComponent {...props} />;
  };
}

function SecretContent() {
  return <div>Secret Content: Only for authorized users!</div>;
}

const AuthorizedContent = withAuthorization(SecretContent);

// Usage in App
function App() {
  return <AuthorizedContent isAuthenticated={false} />;
}
```

**Detailed Explanation**:

1. **withAuthorization HOC**: ‡¶è‡¶á HOC authentication check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `isAuthenticated` prop ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `isAuthenticated` false ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá "You are not authorized to view this content" ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **SecretContent Component**: ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ component, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ authorized users ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ó‡ßã‡¶™‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º content ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
3. **Enhanced Component**: `AuthorizedContent` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `SecretContent` ‡¶ï‡ßá `withAuthorization` HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Usage**: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® `isAuthenticated={false}` ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® user ‡¶ï‡ßá "You are not authorized..." ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ `isAuthenticated` true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ content ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### 6. ‚úÖ Best Practices for HOCs

1. **Descriptive Naming**: HOC ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ meaningful ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º HOC ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `withLoadingIndicator`, `withAuthorization` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§
2. **Don‚Äôt Overuse HOCs**: HOC ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá composition ‡¶¨‡¶æ custom hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
3. **Props Management**: HOC ‡¶è `props` pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá wrapped component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ props ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá pass ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `{...props}` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ props wrapped component ‡¶è ‡¶ö‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
4. **Static Method Copy**: HOCs ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º static methods ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `hoist-non-react-statics` library ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá static methods ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç properties ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
5. **Avoid Side Effects**: HOCs pure function ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶æ wrapped component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã value ‡¶¨‡¶æ state ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

React ‡¶è **Higher Order Components (HOC)** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶∂‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÄ ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modular ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® feature ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logic ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§ HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ application ‡¶ï‡ßá modular, flexible, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ üòÑ

# Chapter-13.1: A Real-World Example of HOC

## Problem Scenario:

‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø element, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‚Äô‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ common logic ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

- Count ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§
- State management ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á logic ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá **HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## Steps to Solve Using HOC:

1. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ count increment ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç state management ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ component (CounterButton ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HoverCounter) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
3. ‡¶è‡¶á component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶§‡ßá HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá logic ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## Step-by-Step Code with Explanation

---

### Step 1: Basic Components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

#### Component 1: CounterButton Component

```javascript
function CounterButton({ count, incrementCount }) {
  return <button onClick={incrementCount}>Button Clicked {count} times</button>;
}

export default CounterButton;
```

#### Component 2: HoverCounter Component

```javascript
function HoverCounter({ count, incrementCount }) {
  return <h2 onMouseOver={incrementCount}>Hovered {count} times</h2>;
}

export default HoverCounter;
```

---

### Step 2: Higher Order Component ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function withCounter(WrappedComponent) {
  return function EnhancedComponent(props) {
    const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

    const incrementCount = () => {
      setCount(count + 1);
    };

    return (
      <WrappedComponent
        count={count}
        incrementCount={incrementCount}
        {...props}
      />
    );
  };
}

export default withCounter;
```

#### ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:

1. **HOC Function**:

   - `withCounter` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø HOC ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø component (`WrappedComponent`) ‡¶ï‡ßá enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   - ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø count ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç increment logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

2. **State Management**:

   - `useState` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `count` state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - `incrementCount` function count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

3. **Props Passing**:
   - `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `incrementCount` props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `WrappedComponent` ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - Original props ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá maintain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `...props` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### Step 3: HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Enhanced Components ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

#### Enhanced CounterButton

```javascript
import CounterButton from "./CounterButton";
import withCounter from "./withCounter";

const EnhancedCounterButton = withCounter(CounterButton);

export default EnhancedCounterButton;
```

#### Enhanced HoverCounter

```javascript
import HoverCounter from "./HoverCounter";
import withCounter from "./withCounter";

const EnhancedHoverCounter = withCounter(HoverCounter);

export default EnhancedHoverCounter;
```

---

### Step 4: App Component ‡¶è Enhanced Components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

```javascript
import React from "react";
import EnhancedCounterButton from "./EnhancedCounterButton";
import EnhancedHoverCounter from "./EnhancedHoverCounter";

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <EnhancedCounterButton />
      <EnhancedHoverCounter />
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

---

## How the HOC Simplifies the Code

### HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Code Reusability**:

   - `withCounter` HOC ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `incrementCount` logic ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶ø‡•§
   - CounterButton ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HoverCounter ‡¶â‡¶≠‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á HOC ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

2. **Separation of Concerns**:

   - HOC state management ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç counting logic ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ components (CounterButton ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HoverCounter) ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ UI ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç event handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

3. **Consistency in Logic**:
   - ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã component ‡¶è count ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç increment logic ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ HOC logic centralize ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### HOC ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßÄ ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã:

1. **Duplicate Logic**:

   - ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è `useState` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `incrementCount` ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§
   - ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá code redundancy ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintenance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§

2. **Difficult Maintenance**:
   - Future ‡¶è logic ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è individually ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§

---

### Detailed Step-by-Step Workflow

1. **WrappedComponent**:

   - HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá `WrappedComponent` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶Ø‡¶æ enhance ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: CounterButton ‡¶¨‡¶æ HoverCounter‡•§

2. **Props Passing**:

   - HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `incrementCount` props `WrappedComponent` ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - Original props retain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `...props` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

3. **Reusable Logic**:

   - Count ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç increment logic ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ HOC ‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

4. **Enhanced Components**:
   - HOC ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá Enhanced Components (EnhancedCounterButton ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç EnhancedHoverCounter) ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior extend ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### Final Output:

- **EnhancedCounterButton**:

  - Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§
  - Output: `Button Clicked 1 times`.

- **EnhancedHoverCounter**:
  - Element hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§
  - Output: `Hovered 1 times`.

---
