# Chapter-14: React Render Props

## Problem Scenario:

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø counter feature ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞:

1. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø element hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø counter feature ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á **logic** (count management) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component-‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á logic ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá code redundancy ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintenance ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

## Solution Using Render Props:

Render Props ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **common logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º**‡•§ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ counting logic ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® UI components-‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

---

## What is Render Props?

React ‡¶è **Render Props** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø pattern ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **function** ‡¶ï‡ßá prop ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á function ‡¶ï‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component ‡¶è‡¶∞ output ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá reusable logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## Implementation of Render Props with Counter

### Step-by-Step Code and Explanation:

---

### Step 1: Create a `Counter` Component with Render Props

#### Counter.js

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Counter({ render }) {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  const increment = () => {
    setCount(count + 1);
  };

  return <div>{render({ count, increment })}</div>;
}

export default Counter;
```

#### Explanation:

1. **State Management**:

   - `useState` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` function handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
   - `count` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® `0` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá count ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§

2. **Render Props**:
   - `Counter` component ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **function** (render prop) ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` props ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - ‡¶è‡¶á render function `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### Step 2: Create UI Components for Click and Hover Counters

#### ClickCounter.js

```javascript
function ClickCounter({ count, increment }) {
  return <button onClick={increment}>Button Clicked {count} times</button>;
}

export default ClickCounter;
```

#### Explanation:

- **UI Rendering**:
  - `ClickCounter` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø button render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Button ‡¶è click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `increment` function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `count` update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

#### HoverCounter.js

```javascript
function HoverCounter({ count, increment }) {
  return <h2 onMouseOver={increment}>Hovered {count} times</h2>;
}

export default HoverCounter;
```

#### Explanation:

- **UI Rendering**:
  - `HoverCounter` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø heading render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
  - Heading ‡¶è hover ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá `increment` function call ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `count` update ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### Step 3: Use the `Counter` Component to Share Logic

#### App.js

```javascript
import React from "react";
import Counter from "./Counter";
import ClickCounter from "./ClickCounter";
import HoverCounter from "./HoverCounter";

function App() {
  return (
    <div>
      <h1>React Render Props Example</h1>

      {/* Click Counter */}
      <Counter
        render={({ count, increment }) => (
          <ClickCounter count={count} increment={increment} />
        )}
      />

      {/* Hover Counter */}
      <Counter
        render={({ count, increment }) => (
          <HoverCounter count={count} increment={increment} />
        )}
      />
    </div>
  );
}

export default App;
```

---

## How Render Props Solves the Problem

### Without Render Props (Problem):

1. **Duplicate Logic**:
   - `ClickCounter` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `HoverCounter` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` logic ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§
2. **Difficult Maintenance**:
   - Future ‡¶è logic ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã‡•§

---

### With Render Props (Solution):

1. **Shared Logic**:

   - `Counter` component logic (count ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç increment) encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   - ‡¶è‡¶á logic render props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `ClickCounter` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `HoverCounter` ‡¶è share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

2. **Separation of Concerns**:
   - `Counter` component logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   - `ClickCounter` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `HoverCounter` UI handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### Final Output:

#### Click Counter:

```
[Button]
Button Clicked 0 times
```

#### Hover Counter:

```
Hovered 0 times
```

---

### Detailed Explanation of the Code Flow:

1. **Counter Component**:

   - `useState` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá count ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç increment logic manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   - `render` prop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

2. **Render Prop Function**:

   - `render` function ‡¶è `count` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `increment` ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
   - UI component (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `ClickCounter`, `HoverCounter`) ‡¶è‡¶á render function ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá props ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

3. **Dynamic UI Creation**:
   - Render Props UI ‡¶ï‡ßá flexible ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
   - `ClickCounter` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `HoverCounter` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### Advantages of Render Props in this Example:

1. **Code Reusability**:
   - Counting logic ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶¨ components ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Logic Encapsulation**:
   - Counting logic `Counter` component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **UI Flexibility**:
   - `render` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ UI ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§
4. **Maintenance-Friendly**:
   - Logic ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ `Counter` component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### üìò Introduction to Context API

React **Context API** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø powerful tool ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data pass ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§, data parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá child component ‡¶è props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá nested structure ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø layer ‡¶è props pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ cumbersome ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá‡•§ **Context API** ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data globally manage ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡•§

Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component tree ‡¶§‡ßá data ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ data ‡¶è‡¶∞ accessibility ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá interaction ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§

---

### üßê Why Use Context API?

Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data share ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central location ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá data ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã nested component ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶á data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Avoids Prop Drilling**: ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã nested component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø layer ‡¶è props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§
2. **Centralized State Management**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã component ‡¶è access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§
3. **Reusability and Flexibility**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á context ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ reusability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexibility ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

Context API ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ data (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® theme, user information, authentication status) global ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá accessible ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§

---

### üîç Core Concepts of Context API

Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **Context Creation**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø container ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

   ```javascript
   const ThemeContext = React.createContext(defaultValue);
   ```

   ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `ThemeContext` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá data provide ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

2. **Provider Component**: Context provider component data ‡¶¨‡¶æ state provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á data ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã child component access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

   ```javascript
   <ThemeContext.Provider value={/* some data */}>
     {/* Child components */}
   </ThemeContext.Provider>
   ```

   Provider component ‡¶è `value` props ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ nested component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

3. **Consumer Component**: Context consumer component ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã nested component context ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
   ```javascript
   <ThemeContext.Consumer>
     {value => /* render something based on the context value */}
   </ThemeContext.Consumer>
   ```
   Consumer component ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá context ‡¶è‡¶∞ data dynamically render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂ Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data share ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç access ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚öôÔ∏è Implementing Context API in React

React ‡¶è Context API implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞ provider component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç consumer component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá context ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø basic ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

#### Example: Implementing Theme Context

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from "react";

// Step 1: Create a Context
const ThemeContext = createContext();

// Step 2: Create a Provider Component
function ThemeProvider({ children }) {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState("light");

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

// Step 3: Create a Component that Consumes the Context
function ThemedButton() {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return (
    <button
      onClick={() => setTheme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light")}
      style={{
        background: theme === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
        color: theme === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
      }}
    >
      Toggle Theme
    </button>
  );
}

// Step 4: Use the Provider in the App Component
function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeProvider>
      <ThemedButton />
    </ThemeProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Context Creation**: `ThemeContext` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ theme ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ data ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Provider Component**: `ThemeProvider` component `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ `theme` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setTheme` value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá context ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Consumer Component**: `ThemedButton` component `useContext` hook ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `ThemeContext` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç button ‡¶è‡¶∞ theme dynamically update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Using the Provider**: `App` component ‡¶è `ThemeProvider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application ‡¶è `theme` context provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø global theme ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã component ‡¶è dynamically access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

---

### üìñ Real-life Examples

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

#### Example 1: User Authentication Context

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø application ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user authentication status check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡•§ Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central authentication context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from "react";

// Create an Authentication Context
const AuthContext = createContext();

function AuthProvider({ children }) {
  const [isAuthenticated, setIsAuthenticated] = useState(false);

  const login = () => setIsAuthenticated(true);
  const logout = () => setIsAuthenticated(false);

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ isAuthenticated, login, logout }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

// Component that Consumes the Auth Context
function UserStatus() {
  const { isAuthenticated, login, logout } = useContext(AuthContext);

  return (
    <div>
      {isAuthenticated ? (
        <>
          <p>User is logged in</p>
          <button onClick={logout}>Logout</button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <p>User is logged out</p>
          <button onClick={login}>Login</button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <AuthProvider>
      <UserStatus />
    </AuthProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **AuthContext Creation**: `AuthContext` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ authentication status ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Provider Component**: `AuthProvider` component ‡¶è `isAuthenticated`, `login`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `logout` method value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Consumer Component**: `UserStatus` component `AuthContext` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `isAuthenticated` status access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç user ‡¶è‡¶∞ login ‡¶¨‡¶æ logout status ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ UI render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Using the Provider**: `App` component ‡¶è `AuthProvider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application ‡¶è authentication context provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central authentication state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

#### Example 2: Language Context for Multilingual Application

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø multilingual application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø language context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ language change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from "react";

// Create a Language Context
const LanguageContext = createContext();

function LanguageProvider({ children }) {
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState("en");

  const switchLanguage = (lang) => setLanguage(lang);

  return (
    <LanguageContext.Provider value={{ language, switchLanguage }}>
      {children}
    </LanguageContext.Provider>
  );
}

// Component that Consumes the Language Context
function LanguageSwitcher() {
  const { language, switchLanguage } = useContext(LanguageContext);

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Current Language: {language}</p>
      <button onClick={() => switchLanguage("en")}>English</button>
      <button onClick={() => switchLanguage("es")}>Spanish</button>
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <LanguageProvider>
      <LanguageSwitcher />
    </LanguageProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **LanguageContext Creation**: `LanguageContext` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ language preference ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Provider Component**: `LanguageProvider` component ‡¶è `language` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `switchLanguage` function provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Consumer Component**: `LanguageSwitcher` component ‡¶è `useContext` hook ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `LanguageContext` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç language switch ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø UI ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Using the Provider**: `App` component ‡¶è `LanguageProvider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application ‡¶è language context provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá, Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central language management system ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™

‡¶õ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ UI change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices for Context API

Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Best Practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá code structure ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

1. **Avoid Overusing Context**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç frequently accessed data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
2. **Use Separate Contexts for Different Data**: ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá code ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
3. **Minimize Re-renders**: Context value change ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá re-render ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶§‡¶æ context ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§
4. **Document Context Usage**: Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º context ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ comments ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç documentation ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

React ‡¶è Context API ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data share ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç accessibility ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular, reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Proper implementation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá React ‡¶è ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ üòä

    <b><a href="#learn-reactjs-in-30-chapters">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>

# Chapter-16: How to Use React Context API

## Table of Contents

- [Overview of Context API](#overview-of-context-api)
- [When to Use Context API](#when-to-use-context-api)
- [Steps to Implement Context API](#steps-to-implement-context-api)

  - [2. Providing the Context](#2-providing-the-context)
  - [3. Consuming the Context](#3-consuming-the-context)
- [Example: Theme Context in a Simple Application](#example-theme-context-in-a-simple-application)

---

### üìò Overview of Context API

React **Context API** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§, React ‡¶è data pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **props drilling** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶†‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® nested component structure ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá data ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø parent ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá deep-nested child component ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ props drilling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üßê When to Use Context API

Context API ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® data ‡¶¨‡¶æ state application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï component ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ use cases:

1. **Authentication State**: Logged-in user ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø application ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
2. **Theme Management**: Light ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dark mode ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ global theme switch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§
3. **Language Preference**: Multilingual applications ‡¶è preferred language context ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§

Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ø‡¶á global level ‡¶è ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®; ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ props ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã‡•§

---

### üîç Steps to Implement Context API

React ‡¶è Context API implement ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

#### 1. Creating a Context

‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `React.createContext()` function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext } from "react";

// Creating a Theme Context
const ThemeContext = createContext();
```

**Explanation**:

- `ThemeContext` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ data ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶á context ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ data globally provide ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

---

#### 2. Providing the Context

Context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **Provider** component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component tree ‡¶§‡ßá provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Provider component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá context data ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶≤ child component ‡¶è accessible ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function ThemeProvider({ children }) {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState("light");

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

export { ThemeProvider, ThemeContext };
```

**Explanation**:

- `ThemeProvider` component `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶ï‡ßá wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `value` prop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- `theme` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setTheme` value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `ThemeContext` ‡¶è pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ child component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶á provider component ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã nested component ‡¶è context data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§

---

#### 3. Consuming the Context

Context data consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **Consumer component** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **useContext hook** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Consumer component ‡¶¨‡¶æ useContext hook ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá child component context ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React, { useContext } from "react";
import { ThemeContext } from "./ThemeProvider";

function ThemedButton() {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return (
    <button
      onClick={() => setTheme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light")}
      style={{
        backgroundColor: theme === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
        color: theme === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
      }}
    >
      Toggle Theme
    </button>
  );
}

export default ThemedButton;
```

**Explanation**:

- `useContext(ThemeContext)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `theme` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setTheme` access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Button ‡¶è‡¶∞ style `theme` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá change ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç click event ‡¶è theme toggle ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### üìñ Example: Theme Context in a Simple Application

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø simple ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø theme context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶§‡¶æ button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá toggle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from "react";

// Step 1: Create a Context
const ThemeContext = createContext();

// Step 2: Create a Provider Component
function ThemeProvider({ children }) {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState("light");

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, setTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

// Step 3: Create a Component that Consumes the Context
function ThemedButton() {
  const { theme, setTheme } = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return (
    <button
      onClick={() => setTheme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light")}
      style={{
        backgroundColor: theme === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
        color: theme === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
      }}
    >
      Toggle Theme
    </button>
  );
}

// Step 4: Use the Provider in the App Component
function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeProvider>
      <ThemedButton />
    </ThemeProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Creating the Context**: `ThemeContext` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ theme data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
2. **Providing the Context**: `ThemeProvider` component `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶ï‡ßá wrap ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `theme` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setTheme` value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Consuming the Context**: `ThemedButton` component `useContext` hook ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `ThemeContext` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá `theme` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `setTheme` access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç button ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá theme toggle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Using the Provider**: `App` component ‡¶è `ThemeProvider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã application ‡¶è theme context provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

**Output**:

- Button click ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá theme light ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá dark ‡¶è ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dark ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá light ‡¶è toggle ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices for Context API

Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ Best Practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá code structure ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

1. **Limit Context Usage to Global Data**: ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ global data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
2. **Use Multiple Contexts for Different Data**: ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ data ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá code ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
3. **Memoize Context Values**: Context value ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá re-renders ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `useMemo` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶®‡•§
4. **Clear Documentation**: Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ comments ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç documentation ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

React ‡¶è‡¶∞ Context API ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá global data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶ï‡ßá modular, reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç flexible ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ Proper implementation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá React ‡¶è ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ üòä

# Chapter-17: React Context API: `contextType` & `useContext` Hook

## Table of Contents

- [Introduction to Context API](#introduction-to-context-api)
- [What is `contextType`](#what-is-contexttype)
- [How to Use `contextType`](#how-to-use-contexttype)

- [Real-life Examples](#real-life-examples)
- [Best Practices](#best-practices)

---

### üìò Introduction to Context API

React **Context API** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø tool ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Context API props drilling ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø central location ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ data management ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Context API ‡¶§‡ßá `Provider` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `Consumer` ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø combined ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá global data sharing ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ concept ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá: **`contextType`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`useContext` hook**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ø context data consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üßê What is `contextType`

`contextType` ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø static property ‡¶Ø‡¶æ class components ‡¶è context data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class component ‡¶è context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® `contextType` property ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá context ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø component ‡¶è access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

#### Syntax of `contextType`

```javascript
class MyComponent extends React.Component {
  static contextType = MyContext;

  render() {
    return <div>Context Value: {this.context}</div>;
  }
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `MyComponent` class ‡¶è `static contextType = MyContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `MyContext` context ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `this.context` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá context ‡¶è‡¶∞ data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### üîç How to Use `contextType`

`contextType` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, context ‡¶ï‡ßá `static contextType` property ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `this.context` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ï context ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç nested ‡¶¨‡¶æ multiple contexts ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ideal ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### Example of `contextType`

```javascript
import React, { createContext, Component } from "react";

// Create a Context
const ThemeContext = createContext("light");

class ThemedComponent extends Component {
  static contextType = ThemeContext;

  render() {
    return (
      <div
        style={{
          backgroundColor: this.context === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
          color: this.context === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
        }}
      >
        Current Theme: {this.context}
      </div>
    );
  }
}

function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value="dark">
      <ThemedComponent />
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Creating the Context**: `ThemeContext` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ default value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `"light"` ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Using `contextType` in Class Component**: `ThemedComponent` class ‡¶è `static contextType = ThemeContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá context data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Rendering Context Data**: `this.context` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá context ‡¶è‡¶∞ current theme dynamically render ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Using the Provider**: `App` component ‡¶è `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá context value ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá `"dark"` pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚öôÔ∏è The `useContext` Hook Explained

**`useContext` hook** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø React hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional components ‡¶è context consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá context data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç props drilling ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶á context ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø data retrieve ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Syntax of `useContext`

```javascript
const contextValue = useContext(MyContext);
```

**Explanation**:

- `useContext` hook ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `MyContext` ‡¶è‡¶∞ data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `useContext` ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ functional components ‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç context ‡¶ï‡ßá props ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

#### Example of `useContext`

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useContext } from "react";

// Create a Context
const ThemeContext = createContext("light");

function ThemedButton() {
  const theme = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return (
    <button
      style={{
        backgroundColor: theme === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
        color: theme === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
      }}
    >
      Current Theme: {theme}
    </button>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value="dark">
      <ThemedButton />
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Creating the Context**: `ThemeContext` context ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ default value `"light"` ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Using `useContext` Hook**: `ThemedButton` component ‡¶è `useContext(ThemeContext)` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá theme value access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Rendering Theme Data**: button ‡¶è‡¶∞ background ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç color `theme` value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Providing the Context**: `App` component ‡¶è `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá theme value `"dark"` set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### üîÑ Comparing `contextType` and `useContext`

| Feature         | `contextType`                             | `useContext`                                 |
| --------------- | ----------------------------------------- | -------------------------------------------- |
| **Usage**       | Only works in class components            | Only works in functional components          |
| **Syntax**      | `static contextType = MyContext`          | `const value = useContext(MyContext)`        |
| **Limitations** | Limited to a single context per component | Supports multiple contexts easily            |
| **When to Use** | For older class-based codebases           | For modern, hook-based functional components |

---

### üìñ Real-life Examples

#### Example 1: Authentication Status with `useContext`

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø application ‡¶è logged-in user ‡¶è‡¶∞ authentication status handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø context API ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `useContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState } from "react";

// Create Auth Context
const AuthContext = createContext();

function AuthProvider({ children }) {
  const [isAuthenticated, setIsAuthenticated] = useState(false);

  const login = () => setIsAuthenticated(true);
  const logout = () => setIsAuthenticated(false);

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ isAuthenticated, login, logout }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

function UserStatus() {
  const { isAuthenticated, login, logout } = useContext(AuthContext);

  return (
    <div>
      {isAuthenticated ? (
        <>
          <p>Welcome back!</p>
          <button onClick={logout}>Logout</button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <p>Please log in.</p>
          <button onClick={login}>Login</button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <AuthProvider>
      <UserStatus />
    </AuthProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Auth Context Creation**: `AuthContext` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ authentication data store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Provider Component**: `AuthProvider` component ‡¶è `isAuthenticated`, `login`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `logout` function provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Consuming Context with `useContext`**: `UserStatus` component ‡¶è `useContext(AuthContext)` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá authentication data access ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

#### Example 2: Using `contextType` for User Preferences in Class Components

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø class component ‡¶è user ‡¶è‡¶∞ preferred language context handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `contextType` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```javascript
import React, { createContext, Component } from "react";

// Create Language Context
const LanguageContext = createContext("en");

class LanguageDisplay extends Component {
  static contextType = LanguageContext;

  render() {
    return (
      <div>
        Preferred Language: {this.context === "en" ? "English" : "Spanish"}
      </div>
    );
  }
}

function App() {
  return (
    <LanguageContext.Provider value="es">
      <LanguageDisplay />
    </LanguageContext.Provider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

**Explanation**:

1. **Creating Language Context**: `LanguageContext` ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç default value `"en"` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
2. **Using `contextType` in Class Component**: `LanguageDisplay` class component ‡¶è `contextType` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `LanguageContext` ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
3. **Accessing Context with `this.context`**: `this.context` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá preferred language dynamically display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
4. **Providing Context**: `App` component ‡¶è `LanguageContext.Provider` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá value `"es"` set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices for Using `contextType` and `useContext`

1. **Use `useContext` for Modern Functional Components**: Functional component ‡¶è `useContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá code ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç concise ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
2. **Use `contextType` in Legacy Class Components**: ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã class component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `contextType` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
3. **Limit Context Usage to Necessary Data**: ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ essential ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç frequently accessed data context ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
4. **Clear Documentation**: Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º `contextType`

‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `useContext` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ comments ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç documentation ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

---

React ‡¶è **`contextType`** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **`useContext`** ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ tool, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Context API ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data sharing ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ `useContext` functional component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá `contextType` class component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßÄ‡•§ Proper usage ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Context API ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü tools ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá React ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç scalable application ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§ üòä

### üìò Introduction to React Hooks

**React Hooks** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã React 16.8 ‡¶è ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø feature ‡¶Ø‡¶æ functional components ‡¶è state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ class components ‡¶è state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle methods ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßã, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Hooks ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ functional components ‡¶è‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá code structure ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ì ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

React Hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modular ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Hooks ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á logic ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ behavior ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üßê Why Use Hooks?

Hooks React ‡¶è‡¶∞ structure ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç code ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **Functional Components Only**: Hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ functional components ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç lifecycle logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ class components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßÇ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2. **Reusable Logic**: Hooks ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á logic ‡¶ï‡ßá reusable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá common logic share ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶ï‡•§
3. **Simplifies Code Structure**: Hooks component structure ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Avoids Prop Drilling**: Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá `useContext` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá nested components ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá data ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá pass ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### üîç Essential React Hooks

#### 1. `useState`

**`useState`** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è state ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø initial state ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á state ‡¶è‡¶∞ current value ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø function ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ state update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const [state, setState] = useState(initialValue);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { useState } from "react";

function Counter() {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {count}</p>
      <button onClick={() => setCount(count + 1)}>Increment</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `count` ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø state variable ‡¶Ø‡¶æ `useState(0)` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá initialize ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `setCount` function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `count` update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ button ‡¶è‡¶∞ click event ‡¶è call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

#### 2. `useEffect`

**`useEffect`** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ side effects handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, DOM update ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶¨‡¶æ timer set ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø component ‡¶è‡¶∞ rendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependency array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá re-run ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
useEffect(() => {
  // Side effect code
}, [dependencies]);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from "react";

function DataFetcher() {
  const [data, setData] = useState(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch("https://api.example.com/data")
      .then((response) => response.json())
      .then((result) => setData(result));
  }, []);

  return <div>{data ? JSON.stringify(data) : "Loading..."}</div>;
}
```

**Explanation**:

- Data fetch ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `useEffect` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component render ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `[]` empty dependency array ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á effect ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ run ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

#### 3. `useContext`

**`useContext`** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ Context API ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá global state ‡¶¨‡¶æ data consume ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø props drilling ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç context ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø data access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const contextValue = useContext(MyContext);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useContext } from "react";

const ThemeContext = createContext("light");

function ThemedComponent() {
  const theme = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return <div>Current Theme: {theme}</div>;
}

function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value="dark">
      <ThemedComponent />
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}
```

**Explanation**:

- `useContext` Hook ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá `ThemeContext` ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá theme value ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- `ThemeContext.Provider` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá `ThemedComponent` context ‡¶è provide ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ value access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

### üîÑ Additional React Hooks

#### 1. `useReducer`

**`useReducer`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø complex state management Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ reducer function ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá state ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dispatch function ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø `useState` ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá complex logic handle ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(reducer, initialState);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { useReducer } from "react";

function reducer(state, action) {
  switch (action.type) {
    case "increment":
      return { count: state.count + 1 };
    case "decrement":
      return { count: state.count - 1 };
    default:
      return state;
  }
}

function Counter() {
  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(reducer, { count: 0 });

  return (
    <div>
      <p>Count: {state.count}</p>
      <button onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "increment" })}>Increment</button>
      <button onClick={() => dispatch({ type: "decrement" })}>Decrement</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

#### 2. `useRef`

**`useRef`** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ component ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá mutable reference ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø DOM element ‡¶è‡¶∞ reference ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ value persist ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const ref = useRef(initialValue);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { useRef } from "react";

function TextInputFocus() {
  const inputRef = useRef(null);

  return (
    <div>
      <input ref={inputRef} type="text" />
      <button onClick={() => inputRef.current.focus()}>Focus Input</button>
    </div>
  );
}
```

---

#### 3. `useMemo`

**`useMemo`** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ computationally expensive function ‡¶è‡¶∞ result ‡¶ï‡ßá cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá rerendering ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º computation ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const memoizedValue = useMemo(() => computeExpensiveValue(a, b), [a, b]);
```

**Example**:

```javascript
import React, { useMemo, useState } from "react";

function ExpensiveCalculationComponent({ number }) {
  const calculatedValue = useMemo(() => {
    return expensiveCalculation(number);
  }, [number]);

  return <div>Calculated Value: {calculatedValue}</div>;
}
```

---

#### 4. `useCallback`

**`useCallback`** ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Hook ‡¶Ø‡¶æ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ instance ‡¶ï‡ßá cache ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç dependency ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á instance ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

**Syntax**:

```javascript
const memoizedCallback = useCallback(() => {
  // Function code
}, [dependencies]);
```

---

### üìñ Real-life Examples

#### Example 1: User Authentication with `useContext` and `useState`

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useContext, useState } from "react";

const AuthContext = createContext();

function AuthProvider({ children }) {
  const [isAuthenticated, setIsAuthenticated] = useState(false);

  const login = () => setIsAuthenticated(true);
  const logout = () => setIsAuthenticated(false);

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ isAuthenticated, login, logout }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

function UserStatus() {
  const { isAuthenticated, login, logout } = useContext(AuthContext);

  return (
    <div>
      {isAuthenticated ? (
        <>
          <p>Welcome, User!</p>
          <button onClick={logout}>Logout</button>
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <p>Please log in.</p>
          <button onClick={login}>Login</button>
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <AuthProvider>
      <UserStatus />
    </AuthProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

#### Example 2: Theme Toggle with `useState` and `useContext`

```javascript
import React, { createContext, useState, useContext } from "react";

const ThemeContext = createContext();

function ThemeProvider({ children }) {
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState("light");

  const toggleTheme = () => set;

  Theme(theme === "light" ? "dark" : "light");

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, toggleTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
}

function ThemedComponent() {
  const { theme, toggleTheme } = useContext(ThemeContext);

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        backgroundColor: theme === "light" ? "#fff" : "#333",
        color: theme === "light" ? "#000" : "#fff",
      }}
    >
      <p>Current Theme: {theme}</p>
      <button onClick={toggleTheme}>Toggle Theme</button>
    </div>
  );
}

function App() {
  return (
    <ThemeProvider>
      <ThemedComponent />
    </ThemeProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
```

---

### ‚úÖ Best Practices for Using Hooks

1. **Use Hooks Only in Functional Components**: Hooks ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ functional components ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
2. **Follow Hook Rules**: Hooks ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá nested structure ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ top-level ‡¶è use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§
3. **Optimize with `useMemo` and `useCallback`**: Expensive computations ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç unnecessary re-renders ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá `useMemo` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `useCallback` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
4. **Use Custom Hooks for Reusable Logic**: Custom Hooks ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá reusable logic encapsulate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§‡•§

React Hooks component structure ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì modular, reusable, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ Proper usage ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç best practices ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Hooks ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá React application ‡¶è ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ performance ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç code clarity ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ üòä
